Current Affairs Commentary

Criticism of Britain on the Issue of Rescuing Silver Prices 41

Since the silver faction in the US Congress under the Roosevelt administration advocated a policy of raising silver prices, some public opinion in China, which uses silver as its monetary standard, has believed that the change in US policy must have an absolutely opposite impact on China's interests. There are two factions for and against the approval of the London Eight-Nation Silver Agreement, and there is even more discussion on the plan to rescue silver prices, as if the rise or fall of silver prices is the key to the entire problem. However, in our view, this kind of disagreement is not enough to be said to have a basic understanding of China's silver problem today.

Silver, as a commodity, is regarded by the United States and other similar countries as the same as ordinary goods on the market. However, our country regards it as the standard for the value of all the wealth of the people. How its price rises and falls abroad not only affects the exchange rate of silver dollars or prices in our country, but also causes different views among all sectors of society on the interests of silver price fluctuations. The Roosevelt administration in the United States suddenly raised silver prices artificially when they had fallen miserably for a long time. There is no need to say how much it can harm our society and disrupt our finances. From the perspective of stabilizing society and promoting commerce, today's public opinion in our country advocates stabilizing the world silver market as a prerequisite, or even achieving the stability of our country's currency exchange rate. This is also the highest principle at present. However, the center of the problem lies elsewhere. That is, first, whether China's current financial organization can execute the purpose of stabilizing the foreign exchange rate under a certain plan. Second, whether the central government's current financial situation is sufficient to assume the responsibility of stabilizing the exchange rate. If both are impossible, then when the United States manipulates the silver market, our country will only be at the mercy of others and be in an absolutely passive position. If, under such circumstances, we talk highly about how to rescue silver prices, and even that the impact of silver prices is enough to cause absolute gains and losses, how can we explore the origins?

Looking at the past, when silver prices first fell in 1929, everyone in the country was troubled by the excessive fall in silver. Now that silver prices are about to rise, everyone is afraid again. Between gains and losses, they have failed to see the power of the central authorities and have failed to recognize the current financial organization. Therefore, there is no standard to speak of in the midst of joy and fear. Originally, the change in silver prices had no absolute standard for determining how much benefit or harm it would bring to us. When silver rises from cheap to expensive, domestic industrial capital is indeed under considerable pressure, and those who rely on gold coin income for their livelihoods have also suffered considerable losses (assuming that silver is expensive in relation to gold). However, at the same time, foreign goods are cheaper, and the burden on consumers is reduced. If it can be used to develop national construction undertakings, it may be enough to offset the harm of expensive silver. The reduction of foreign debt principal and interest is just a side effect. On the contrary, when silver goes from expensive to cheap, although it feels difficult to build and foreign debt increases daily, industries can be developed from this. Benefits and harms cannot be absolutely separated. From this point of view, when silver prices are uncertain, what is valuable is that the government and the people can implement a certain policy. Otherwise, the high or low price of silver is enough to bring endless worries to the country. The failure to actively develop the people's industry when silver was cheap after 1929 is the same as not necessarily doing anything when silver is expensive in the future. So, what is this certain policy? It is the stability of the central government's finances and the strengthening of the financial organization. These two things are already done. Only by understanding this can we discuss the impact of silver prices.

Relaxation of Japanese-Russian Relations 42

Observations by American Political Circles

(Washington) Senior US government officials are now gradually believing that Japan and Russia may be able to safely pass through the end of 1934 without resorting to arms. In the past week or two, the view held in official circles was that the Japanese-Russian war would break out around the first half of 1934, or even in the spring of 1934. This view can be seen in general in the declaration of Congressman Lenane three weeks ago. Lenane stated in his declaration that he hoped that the Japanese-Russian war would not be launched in the spring. Political observers seem to agree with the view that the trend of war and peace between Japan and Russia is shifted by the policies of the two countries in Manchuria. It is recognized here that the recent release of six Russian officials of the Chinese Eastern Railway by the "Manchukuo" government is a sign that the situation between Japan and Russia is gradually tending towards relaxation. Since the Soviet Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov issued a declaration on December 29, 1933, condemning Japan for preparing for war against Russia, there have been many improvements in the situation between Japan and Russia. It is stated here that the purpose of the large amount of machinery and equipment currently purchased by Soviet Russian representatives in the United States is to revitalize Soviet Russian industry and commerce. However, this kind of industry is related to war preparations. Soviet Russian purchasing agents in the United States are very close to aircraft manufacturing factories, and it is said that they will specialize in ordering aircraft engines. Moreover, the purchase of machinery is also an important item in the Soviet Russian purchase list. This kind of machinery will include machines used to manufacture automobiles, nitrogen, and mining machines. (16th National Telegraph)

Results of the Rome Conference Italy, Austria, and Hungary Sign Agreement 43

Including Economic and Political Matters

Not Refusing the Participation of France, Germany, and Other Countries

Premier Mussolini's Policy Initially Successful

Austria and Hungary Obtain an Outlet to the Adriatic Sea

Italy Does Not Want Central Europe to be Dominated by Any Country

Rome The agreement between Italy, Austria, and Hungary was signed at 4:00 PM today by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss, and Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös. The agreement consists of two items, one for political events and one for economic events. It is reported that the agreement declares Austria's independence and the intention of the signatory countries to cooperate in order to promote the economic progress of the Danube countries, and invites other countries such as France, Germany, and the Little Entente to join this agreement. Prime Minister Mussolini has always held a firm position, not wanting Central Europe to be dominated by any country. Although the agreement signed today may involve economic concessions from Italy, this can be seen as a victory for Prime Minister Mussolini's advocacy of moderating Central Europe. (17th Reuters Telegraph)

Rome The trilateral meeting between Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös, and Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss, lasted for three hours, starting at 2:00 PM. It is rumored that the three countries will sign two conventions on political and economic matters tomorrow. It is said that the signing of this convention is the result of the first step of Prime Minister Mussolini's new policy. Mussolini's new policy is to avoid meetings attended by countries around the world, and instead consult with one or two neighboring countries separately to reach an agreement, because the convening of world conferences is both difficult and fruitless.

(17th National Telegraph)

Rome Prime Minister Mussolini and Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss and Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös, met again today, ending the political and economic issues discussed yesterday, and initialed two protocols, which will be formally signed tomorrow. The negotiations started by the three prime ministers this week have come to an end. The authorities of the three countries are very satisfied with the results, but as of now, there has been no official statement on the content. Some say that an economic agreement will be signed at the end of the trilateral meeting tomorrow. This agreement, following the Italian principle, is signed separately with Austria and Hungary, not a joint agreement between the three parties. This bilateral treaty will provide special convenience for the commerce of Austria and Hungary, so that they can enjoy the two ports of "Trieste" (belonged to Austria before the war, and was assigned to Italy by the peace treaty) and "Fiume". In addition to the economic agreement, a political declaration will also be issued soon, clearly expressing the guarantee of Austria and Hungary's independence. (16th Hans Telegraph)

Rome The two protocols initialed by the Italian, Austrian, and Hungarian prime ministers today will be formally signed at 4:00 PM tomorrow. The nature of the two protocols is one economic and one political. The latter, in this conversation, has surpassed the economic nature and occupies the primary position. This political protocol does not link the three countries into a close group, but agrees to confirm the commonality of the interests of Italy, Austria, and Hungary, and the necessity of continued cooperation. Under this meaning, this protocol contains the same meaning as the Four-Power Pact, and on the other hand, all countries related to the balance of power in Central Europe are also invited to participate, and to work together with the three contracting countries. Furthermore, this protocol does not stipulate that the territorial clauses in the peace treaty can be modified in the future. Hungarian public opinion is already satisfied with this protocol, and German public opinion is also comforted by it. (17th Havas Telegraph)

Rome The talks between the prime ministers of Italy, Austria, and Hungary have resulted in a Danube agreement covering political and economic spheres. According to this agreement, Italy will give preferential treatment to Austrian grains and certain industrial products and timber from Austria, while Austria and Hungary will give preferential treatment to Italian exports, most of which are manufactured goods. Both Austria and Hungary will enjoy convenient access to the sea at "Trieste" and "Fiume". It is heard from some sources that the three countries have agreed to coordinate actions with each other on certain prescribed political issues, but the statement that the three countries will conclude a commercial agreement has not been confirmed. The Italian side is extremely willing for the three Little Entente countries of Czechoslovakia, Yugoslavia, and Romania and Germany to understand the open nature of this agreement, because Italy and other countries all have the sincerity to seek the cooperation of the Little Entente countries and Germany. What Italy is most concerned about is the independence of the Danube countries, and any action of a hegemonic nature is unacceptable to Italy. (17th Reuters Telegraph)

Rome Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss left his residence at 7:00 this morning and flew to the port of Naples. He will still return to Rome in the afternoon to participate in the trilateral meeting and formally sign the two protocols, political and economic. It is heard that the economic protocol is not a detailed agreement, so some experts from Austria and Hungary are still staying in Rome and are not returning to their countries with Dollfuss and Gömbös. In short, Austrian expert Hiller, the president of the central bank, will return here before Easter to detail the economic agreement that has already been started. (17th Havas Telegraph)

Russian Newspaper Discusses the Situation in Central Europe 44

(Moscow) *Izvestia* commented on the trips of Dollfuss and Gömbös to Rome, saying that the focus of the Rome negotiations was not on economics but on other aspects. Although the Italian press denied this, it could not conceal the truth. Previously, Habicht, the leader of the Austrian National Socialist Party, had issued an ultimatum to the Austrian government, but it had come to naught. This was none other than due to the resolute attitude adopted by the Italian government. If necessary, Italy would not hesitate to defend Austria's independence by force. Paris and Rome were trying to rely on the Rome negotiations to ease the divergence between the Little Entente and Italian policies. However, in our opinion, such negotiations will not have much effect. At most, these negotiations can serve as a way for each to explain their position, but they are by no means steps that can determine the fate of the Danube and Balkan countries. These issues cannot be resolved through diplomacy. (TASS dispatch on the 16th)

Political Truce in France 45

Parliament Declares a Two-Month Recess

Premier Doumergue Will Exercise Broad Powers

Readjusting Tax Regulations and Strictly Implementing Austerity

(Paris) The French Parliament today declared a two-month recess. During this recess, Premier Doumergue and his cabinet will exercise governmental affairs with dictatorial power. The dove of peace has once again come to the "French political battlefield," because Doumergue, formerly known as "Happy President" and now known as "Happy Premier," has completed his thirty-seven days in office under the slogan of "political truce and appeal to public opinion." The Senate and the Chamber of Deputies will grant Premier Doumergue broad powers during the recess, which is a first for the French Parliament. This power includes increasing or decreasing tariffs and drastically tightening the national budget. Doumergue's previous cabinet had been dissolved multiple times due to disputes with Parliament over this power. Before the Chamber of Deputies reconvenes, it intends to hand over these matters entirely to Doumergue. (National Telegram on the 17th)

Portugal Denies Ceding Island to Britain 46

(Paris) The *London Sunday Express* reported on the 11th of this month that the island of Timor in the South Seas, jointly administered by Portugal and the Netherlands, was to be bought by the British government, and that the sale price was between five and ten million pounds. The British government formally denied this the next day. Recently, the Portuguese embassy here also issued a formal declaration, saying that the report that the Portuguese colony was sold to Britain was completely unfounded. (Havas dispatch on the 16th)

Anglo-French Dispute Over Disarmament, Little Hope for British Mediation 47

Germany Has Already Demanded an Air Force

France Has Rejected the British Plan

(Paris) The French cabinet will finally pass the French disarmament note tomorrow. It is said that the note will declare in a moderate but firm tone that the British government's disarmament plan is not sufficient and that the guarantees for management and implementation are particularly incomplete. It is widely believed that since Germany has destroyed the disarmament plan with its demand for thousands of aircraft, and France has this note, the British plan will be stillborn. (Reuters dispatch on the 16th)

France Consistently Upholds the League of Nations 48

No Disarmament Without Guaranteed Security

(Paris) The Senate Foreign Affairs Committee met, and its chairman, Bérenger, based on various diplomatic documents from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, explained the international situation. On Wednesday and Thursday, he met with Foreign Minister Barthou regarding various memorandums related to the disarmament issue, and briefly described the conversation between the two at that time. After a long discussion, the Foreign Affairs Committee drafted a motion, which was passed in full and will be immediately sent to Premier Doumergue and Foreign Minister Barthou. The content of the motion states that (after the Senate discussed the question of diplomatic issues on January 18 of this year, it passed a motion with a majority of 257 votes to 3 votes. (According to this motion, it advocates faithfully adhering to the Covenant of the League of Nations and the Locarno Treaty, and trusts the government to engage in peaceful construction within the scope of the League of Nations, so that France and other countries can become closer in their national relations, and consolidate national defense and security.) The Senate still faithfully adheres to this motion. It also states that the Senate has repeatedly issued declarations in the past, stating that when Germany re-arms and there is no organized security internationally, if there is any international convention that is sufficient to force France to reduce its armaments or abandon the conditions that are indispensable for its national security, France should not be bound by it. The Senate has always faithfully adhered to this declaration and will never change it," and so on. (Havas dispatch on the 15th)

Collecting Materials on National Defense Budgets 49

League of Nations Receives Documents from Forty-One Countries

(Geneva) The National Defense Expenditure Committee of the Disarmament Conference collected documents from various governments regarding their respective budgetary systems and national defense expenditures, and submitted them to the technical committee for study in March 1932. The first task of the committee was to study the documents sent by nineteen countries, and the results were reported in the spring of 1933 and sent to the National Defense Expenditure Committee and the General Committee for review. On January 17 of this year, the technical committee began to study the documents of the other forty-one countries participating in the Disarmament Conference, and this was completed today. For each issue, a comprehensive statement is made based on the collected materials, which will soon be sent to the governments of the countries concerned to solicit their opinions.

(Havas dispatch on the 16th)

Treacherous Winds and Waves in the Atlantic, British Naval Exercise Interrupted 50

Fleet Shelters in the Strait of Gibraltar

Several Ships Sustain Serious Mechanical Damage

Madrid The British naval fleet began naval exercises near Gibraltar on March 11, with the Home Fleet and the Mediterranean Fleet conducting simulated battles. Recently, the news agency here received a telegram from Algeciras (a southern Spanish port) stating that a British fleet consisting of 139 warships had stopped the exercises due to bad weather and sheltered in the Strait of Gibraltar. In addition, three aircraft carriers and two armored ships were moored in the harbor of Algeciras due to their excessive displacement. According to the sailors on the ships, the winds and waves at sea were treacherous, and the fleet was extremely inconvenienced. Several of the ships also sustained serious mechanical damage. The Opium Scourge in the Northeast 51

Designated Planting Areas Publicly Announced

(Changchun) The areas designated for planting opium in "Manchukuo" this year have been decided upon after research by the parties concerned, and various preparations have been completed. However, in Jilin Province, due to the significant relationship with maintaining law and order, the Ministry of Civil Affairs further consulted with the parties concerned. The provincial government issued the following instructions regarding the permitted areas: When maintaining law and order, planting may be prohibited in dense forests and mountainous areas when it is considered an obstacle. Select areas with good law and order and the ability to crack down on planting, gather the planting area determined by the group, and strive to obtain a sufficient harvest. Clearly define the permitted and prohibited areas in the designated counties, and jointly and strictly crack down on them by the Law and Order Maintenance Association and other relevant agencies. Within the permitted counties, cancel the permit or permit the planting area for each household based on the above guidelines, and seek appropriate and proper methods. (Dentsu dispatch on the 17th)

League of Nations Pays Attention to the Pseudo-State's Drug Trade 52

Notifies Countries to Provide Information

Maintains Resolution of Non-Recognition

Avoids Using the Term "Manchukuo"

(London) The issue of opium and other narcotics is now being addressed by the League of Nations. Today, the Secretariat has issued a notice to all countries that can collect necessary information, including the United States and Russia, requesting them to provide information on the production, sale, and use of opium and other narcotics in Manchuria and Jehol, i.e., the so-called "Manchu Empire," as well as detailed information on the illegal drug trade, in accordance with the recommendations of the Opium Advisory Committee. The Advisory Committee stated that the use of the term "Manchukuo" might imply tacit recognition of this new country. Therefore, the term Manchuria and Jehol is used in the notice. (Reuters dispatch on the 17th)

Serious Labor Unrest in the United States 62

Government Tries Hard to Salvage

The Market Has Been Affected

(Washington) The U.S. government is said to be making good progress in averting serious strikes in the nation's key industries, and the government will strive to avert a general strike in another industry. Many railroad directors, in a petition submitted to President Roosevelt today, expressed their agreement with the President's demand to stop "wage reductions for railway employees" in the past six months. According to various railway companies, in addition to the 10% "wage reduction" currently being implemented, a 5% "wage reduction" will be negotiated this month, and this new rule will be implemented from July 1. However, it is widely believed that this matter will not take effect, because at a time when various industrialists are increasing wages for workers or attempting to increase wages, the government will not allow any industrial organization to make unilateral reductions. The strike by automobile industry employees, originally scheduled to be held today, has now been postponed until after the meeting between the National Automobile Manufacturers Association and National Recovery Administrator Johnson. The meeting between Johnson and the National Automobile Manufacturers Association will be held on Tuesday. According to labor leaders, if the meeting does not reach a satisfactory agreement, a strike will be called on Wednesday. It is said that the focus of the conflict is that automobile industry employers do not recognize workers' organizations and unions, while workers demand working hours, wages, and other issues. The company intends to negotiate directly with the unions affiliated with the American Federation of Labor. The company authorities not only refused this consultation, but further organized company groups to resist. Recently, the National Automobile Manufacturers Association suggested increasing wages and reducing working hours, but this suggestion was not accepted by other companies except for Ford Motor Company. It is said that the automobile industry is currently in the peak season, because the orders received in March exceed the company's manufacturing volume. The impact of the strike on the stock market in the past two weeks is like a "dark cloud in the clear sky." The chairman of the American Federation of Labor issued a similar threatening statement, saying that if the automobile industry companies cannot accept the workers' demands, an unprecedented large-scale strike is feared to be imminent. (National Telegram on the 16th)

Catalonia, Spain Declares Temporary Alert 64

Prevent Power Workers' Strike from Causing Disturbances

Barcelona A temporary alert order was declared throughout Catalonia, Spain today. According to this order, the civil governor does not need to transfer his rights to the military and can conscript the army to cope with the situation caused by the continued strike of power plant employees. The current situation is quite serious and contains the possibility of major disturbances. All power plants are currently managed and defended by soldiers. It is reported that strikers in the Tanasa area have threatened municipal workers to prevent them from lighting street lights. It is expected that power plant and railway workers everywhere will start a strike at midnight tonight. (Reuters dispatch on the 17th)

Trial of Assassination Attempt on Italian Prime Minister Opens 65

Rome On June 25 of last year, someone placed a bomb in St. Peter's Church in an attempt to assassinate Prime Minister Mussolini. At that time, suspects Sianka and his son and two others were arrested. The trial was opened by a military court today. Armed troops and Blackshirt personnel were on strict alert around the court. The defendants Sianka and the other three initially strongly denied attempting to assassinate the Prime Minister, saying that the bombing was only a demonstration by anti-fascist groups and was not intended to harm him. After repeated questioning, Sianka confessed that he had prepared to use bombs and poison gas bombs to assassinate the Prime Minister. This plot was agreed upon by them in Paris. It is said that those who plot to assassinate the Prime Minister should be sentenced to death. Therefore, officials believe that three of the defendants will be executed, and the remaining one, named Capaiso, will be sentenced to twenty years in prison. (Reuters on the 16th)

Oxford-Cambridge Boat Race Results 66

Cambridge Wins Over Oxford

(London) Cambridge won the Oxford-Cambridge boat race today. Cambridge has won eleven consecutive times, for a total of 45 wins, while Oxford has won 40 times. (Reuters dispatch on the 17th)

Russian Scientific Report on Stratospheric Exploration Published 67

Composition of the Stratosphere

Not Much Different from the Earth's Atmosphere

Leningrad The astronomical observatory here today published a final report on the scientific achievements of the first stratospheric exploration. The report has extremely interesting discoveries about the composition of the air in the stratosphere. It is said that at an altitude of 57,000 feet, the composition of the air is 20.95% oxygen, while the composition of nitrogen and Nobel's inert gas is not much different from that in the gas layer near the Earth. This difference is really unexpected, because scientists used to believe that the composition of the gas in the stratosphere must be very different from the atmosphere surrounding the Earth. (National Telegram on the 16th)

Page 9

[Missing Beginning of Headline] Tibetan Army Commits Offense, Situation in Xikang Serious

Liu Wenhui Telegraphs that Tibetan Army Illegally Crosses Tongtian River

Delegates from Xikang Meeting at Aida Present Four Demands

Delegates from Xikang Refute Reasonably and Are Almost Detained

Xikang News: The situation in Xikang and Tibet has suddenly become serious. According to recent news from the front, the Tibetan army, using the monks and soldiers of the Da Jin Temple as their vanguard, circumvented and illegally crossed the Jinsha River on Lunar New Year's Eve (February 13th). They confronted our defending troops for two days. Seeing that our forces were weak and difficult to support, they increased the majority of their forces at dawn on February 15th and fiercely attacked Dengke County City on the east bank of the Jinsha River, cutting off the traffic between Dengke and Dege. Only one company of troops was stationed in Dengke City. Due to the disparity in numbers, they immediately withdrew. The Tibetan army then occupied the city. Deng Rang, brigade commander of the 2nd Brigade of the Sichuan-Xikang Army, upon receiving the report, immediately dispatched Regiment Commander Zhang Werong to reinforce. On the 16th, the two sides officially made contact at a strategic pass between Dengke and Dege. The Tibetan soldiers were unable to resist and retreated towards Dengke. Our army arrived near Dengke City on the same day. On the 17th, Dengke was recaptured. The two sides engaged in a fierce melee and charge. As a result, our army gradually regained its original positions. The Tibetan army and the monks and soldiers of the Da Jin Temple retreated in disarray to concentrate at Guanyin Temple. This was at noon on the 17th. The terrain of Guanyin Temple is strategic. The Tibetan army relies on bunkers in that place to defend stubbornly. Our army initially selected a daredevil team to charge, throwing grenades, but the bunkers were solid, easy to defend and difficult to attack. After a stalemate of several days, only over a hundred enemy soldiers were injured, and Guanyin Temple could not be officially recaptured. Later, Zhang Guo dispatched a company each of mortars and mountain guns, rushing to assist in the attack. It is expected that it will be captured within days. Because Guanyin Temple is isolated on the west bank of the Jinsha River, Dengke cannot be captured in a day if Guanyin Temple cannot be captured in a day. At the same time, in the Dege area, the two sides also officially made contact from the 17th. The Tibetan army used machine guns and cannons to cover a large number of leather boats, attempting to force a crossing of the river. Fortunately, our side had built solid fortifications on the east bank, and the Tibetan army calmly resisted when it attacked, sinking many leather boats. The Tibetan side ultimately did not succeed. However, the Tibetan army's offense against Xikang has been prepared for a long time. Now that it has officially launched, their numbers are large and ours are small. Although our side has achieved a temporary victory, the future is still uncertain. Later, Tang Ying and Deng Rang jointly telegraphed Liu Wenhui, Commander-in-Chief of the Sichuan-Xikang Border Defense, requesting reinforcements as soon as possible. After receiving the telegram, Liu reported to all parties on the 23rd and issued a circular telegram on the 25th. In addition to detailing the battle situation at the front, he briefly stated that the enemy army had brazenly started the war, and the war had spread horizontally. It was Wenhui's responsibility to fight hard to defend the border. However, the actual food and funds were already extremely difficult in peacetime. During this military period, it was by no means something that a poor area could handle. He hoped that a comprehensive allocation would be given quickly to avoid mistakes. It is heard that Shi Qingyang, Chairman of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, has sent a telegram to Ya'an, still urging Liu to do his best to avoid military action and advocating a peaceful resolution. However, the Tibetan army has made up its mind to commit offenses against Xikang and has been instigated by a certain imperialist. Now that the two sides have met in battle, if one wants to turn hostility into friendship, one must, of course, satisfy their desires.

As for the purpose of the Tibetan side, it can be seen in the recent Aida meeting. Earlier, Galun Zhendong, stationed in Changdu, Tibet, previously sent his collaborator Xie Jiao, accompanied by translator Cai Jiarong, to Xikang. He then went to Ya'an to visit Liu Wenhui, stating that the Tibetan side had recently lost the Dalai Lama, and Silon Gasha continued to preside over the political and religious power. They have now decided to support the central government and jointly defend against the pressure of foreign forces. The disputes between Tibet and Xikang in recent years have also had a considerable impact on the relationship between the Han and Tibetans. Now, they have decided to make concessions to Xikang and have sent Qiong Rang, a representative familiar with the situation in Xikang and Tibet, to Aida to negotiate with the representatives of the Sichuan-Xikang army. At the same time, the three major temples of Lhasa have also sent representatives to participate in the matter, requesting Liu to send another representative. At that time, Liu was just because the Tibetan side was preparing to invade urgently, and he sent Jiang Yuwen, the negotiator of Kangzang and magistrate of Dege, to depart from Dege, cross the river to Aida, pay condolences to the Dalai Lama, and spy on the reality of the Tibetan army. After Jiang arrived in Aida, Qiong Rang's representative and the representatives of the three major temples also went one after another. Jiang and Qiong Rang were both drafters of the Kangzang peace and war agreement in the past. Unexpectedly, this time they met, Qiong Rang put on a stern face and completely overturned the Kangzang peace treaty. The two sides formally met on February 8th. Qiong Rang then put forward the following four conditions, which were even more demanding than the previous repeated requests from the Tibetan side. The conditions are as follows: (1) Dege (including Dengke, Shiqu Baiyu counties, etc.), Ganzi, Zhanhua, Zhuwo (a village belonging to Luhuo County), and Yan Well in southern Kang, and Hexi villages belonging to Ba'an County must be completely handed over to the jurisdiction of the Tibetan side. (2) The ceasefire agreement signed by both sides in Kangzang in Gangtuo last year should be invalid, and the Sichuan-Xikang army should not be allowed to invoke it again. (3) The monks of the Da Jin Temple have been wandering without a home since they retreated across the Jinsha River to the west bank last year. The Sichuan-Xikang army should now unconditionally allow them to return to the temple and must not deliberately obstruct them. (4) If the Sichuan-Xikang army does not allow the monks of the Da Jin Temple to return to the temple, they will take free action, and the Tibetan side cannot be held responsible. Jiang reasonably refuted, briefly stating that Dege Ganza and Hexi areas of Ba'an are areas belonging to Xikang, and the Sichuan-Xikang military authorities have no right to freely cede them. If the central government explicitly orders them to be ceded to the Tibetan side, they will, of course, comply. If they have not obtained the consent of the central government, the Sichuan-Xikang army cannot give up an inch of Xikang land. If the Tibetan side has this request, they can directly submit it to the central government. The Gangtuo agreement was negotiated by the representatives of both sides in Kangzang and has been approved by the central government. It should now be jointly observed. If a new agreement is to be signed, it should also be based on this standard. How can it be overturned in one day? The monks of the Da Jin Temple have caused chaos for years, and the continuous wars between Kangzang and the joint result of both sides, the temple is also difficult to escape its blame. Last year, the Sichuan-Xikang army drove them out of the country. It was also because the crime deserved it. The Sichuan-Xikang army did not investigate the past and allowed them to return to the temple, which was already a sign of generosity. As for limiting them from bringing firearms into the country, it was also the authorities' punishment for the past and a precautionary measure. If the Tibetan army secretly helps them to cause chaos, the Tibetan army should bear the responsibility. The two sides debated for a long time on the 8th, 9th, 10th and 13th without any concrete results. The Tibetan side even planned to detain Jiang. Later, with the mediation of the representatives of the three major temples, it was decided that the representatives of both sides should ask their respective superiors for instructions. Jiang had just returned to Dege when the Kangzang war suddenly broke out. It is feared that it will not be easy to resolve in a short time. (China United Press)

Premier Sun's Thought and Personality 104

—Chiang's Speech at the Memorial Service for Premier Sun's Death Anniversary—

Nanchang Correspondence: The Jiangxi Provincial Party Headquarters convened representatives from various sectors at 10:00 AM on the 12th in the flower garden at the entrance of the main hall to hold a memorial meeting for the ninth anniversary of Premier Sun's passing. Attendees included Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, Zhang Xueliang, Ding Chao, Wu Shixui, Yang Yongtai, He Guoguang, members of the Provincial Party Headquarters and the Provincial Government, and representatives from various sectors, totaling approximately 600 people. The entire group stood in a circle, led by Chiang Kai-shek in performing the memorial ceremony. Immediately following, he delivered a speech, elaborating on Premier Sun's fundamental thoughts and revolutionary personality throughout his life. The entire audience stood attentively, and the atmosphere was solemn. The meeting concluded around noon with music and a group photograph. The recorded transcript of Chiang's speech is as follows:

"Fellow comrades, today is the memorial day for our Premier's passing. Nine years ago today, at this very moment, our Premier passed away in Beiping. As we commemorate the Premier's death today, we should remember his final call: 'Peace, Struggle, Save China.' This is what the Premier told us: We must overthrow imperialism and complete the National Revolution to save China. We must use peaceful methods, unite in spirit, and make concerted efforts to sacrifice for the country, fighting to the end. Today, as we recall the Premier's last words, 'Peace, Struggle, Save China,' we can understand the revolutionary environment at that time and the Premier's difficult and arduous struggle. From this, we can recognize the Premier's great revolutionary personality. Furthermore, in the weeks before the Premier's passing, Mr. Dai Jitao once asked the Premier about the philosophical foundation of his revolutionary doctrine. Mr. Dai also reported his own research findings on this issue to the Premier. After he finished speaking, the Premier said, 'Your understanding is correct. My revolutionary philosophy is the Philosophy of People's Livelihood.' It was on this occasion that the Premier systematically and concisely imparted his revolutionary philosophy to us. Subsequently, Mr. Dai, based on the Premier's meaning and his own research, wrote a book titled 'The Philosophical Foundation of Sun Wenism,' and specially included a 'Systematic Chart of the Philosophy of People's Livelihood' with an additional explanation as the conclusion of the entire book. Today, as we commemorate the Premier here, each and every one of us should firmly believe in the Premier's revolutionary doctrine, deeply understand the Premier's great revolutionary personality, and genuinely become a follower of the Premier. To do so, we must first clearly understand the origin of the Premier's revolutionary thought, the entire revolutionary personality of the Premier, and the foundation upon which his career was built. Therefore, today I will explain the principles of the Philosophy of People's Livelihood based on the explanations in the Systematic Chart of the Philosophy of People's Livelihood, and share them with all the comrades in Nanchang.

The original explanation states, 'Those who study Sun Yat-senism should first know nine things. First, "The fundamental thought of Mr. Sun is entirely rooted in the Doctrine of the Mean, the orthodox thought of China. Mr. Sun is truly the great sage who inherits the past and opens up the future in the moral culture of China after Confucius."' This first point is about recognizing the source of Premier Sun's thought and his highest position in the history of Chinese culture and morality, pointing out that the Premier is the modern great sage who inherited the orthodox thought of China.

Second, "Mr. Sun's knowledge includes the latest modern science, and he always uses modern scientific methods to solve all problems." This second point is about Premier Sun's thought and learning. In terms of the source of his thought, it naturally inherited the orthodox thought of China throughout history, namely the Doctrine of the Mean since Confucius and Mencius. However, in terms of the scope of his learning, especially the method of solving all practical problems, it actually includes the latest modern science. This is why he became the greatest sage of modern times. We know that if a person only knows the Doctrine of the Mean of the ancients and does not understand the latest science, and cannot use scientific methods to solve all practical problems, then that is a bookworm. Premier Sun's fundamental thought and learning truly spanned the past and the present, encompassing both China and the West, thereby crystallizing into his revolutionary doctrine and manifesting into his revolutionary cause.

Third, "The principles of Mr. Sun's Three Principles of the People are all included within the Principle of People's Livelihood. All his works can be collectively named the Philosophy of People's Livelihood." This third point is to point out that the Three Principles of the People take the Principle of People's Livelihood as the center, and all of Premier Sun's writings can be summarized as the Philosophy of People's Livelihood. The Premier once said, "People's livelihood is the center of history." This sentence is the Premier's final conclusion in his study of history, and it is also a basic theorem of the Philosophy of People's Livelihood. Revolutionary doctrine is originally the highest principle of using human power to conform to and control history. Since people's livelihood is the center of history, the Philosophy of People's Livelihood is the foundation of revolutionary thought. If we want to understand the fundamental system of Premier Sun's thought, we must pay special attention to the study of the Philosophy of People's Livelihood.

Fourth, "Mr. Sun's lifelong efforts were all to save the country and the people through revolutionary means, to break all dreams of individualism, and to realize the Three Principles of the People." This means that Premier Sun's lifelong efforts were to save the country and the nation through revolutionary means. Where does the Premier's revolutionary means lie? It is to break all illusions of individualism, that is, all selfish and self-interested attempts. Because selfish and self-interested individualism is harmful to the entire country and nation, if we want to save the country and the nation, we must thoroughly eradicate this kind of thought and action, and then we can realize Premier Sun's Three Principles of the People to save the country and the nation.

Fifth, "The original purpose of the Three Principles of the People is to restore the nation's self-confidence. Because if the nation's self-confidence cannot be restored, then this weak and large ancient cultural nation, its aging and illness cannot be saved. All new activities cannot be generated. Even if they occur, they do not escape the state of illness and cannot save the nation from peril." This passage is about the fundamental purpose of the Three Principles of the People, which is to awaken the masses and restore the confidence of the general public in their own nation, to understand that our Chinese nation not only possesses the national spirit of self-reliance and independence, but also possesses the superior intelligence of creativity and invention, and even more so, the inherent virtue of peace, righteousness, and supreme greatness. We have a glorious history of five thousand years and a beautiful culture. We are truly an ancient civilized country and an excellent nation. No matter when, no matter how critical the situation, as long as we can restore our inherent national spirit and intelligence, we can certainly promote the glorious history of our nation, build our truly independent and free new country, and open up a long-lasting new life for our entire national civilization. In any case, we cannot be subjected to the oppression and aggression of imperialism, especially not to abandon ourselves and forget the great spirit and glorious history left to us by our ancestors. We must always remember how great our ancestors were and how strong our country has always been. Can't we do now what our ancestors could do before? Each of us must have this confidence and understand that our Chinese nation is not to be bullied at will. Now that people are bullying us, we don't need to be afraid. We must restore the inherent spirit, virtue, and intelligence of the nation to overthrow imperialism and build a brilliant Republic of China.

Sixth, "The method of implementing the Three Principles of the People lies in the common effort of the entire nation to complete the National Revolution, to concentrate the effort of the Chinese National Revolution, and to use state capitalism as the foundation for building the Republic of China." This article discusses the method of implementing the Three Principles of the People. The first step is to awaken the masses so that the entire nation can unite and work together for the revolution. The second step is to complete the National Revolution, which here refers to unifying the country with revolutionary force. The third step is to concentrate the power of the people and the revolutionary party across the country, aiming at state capitalism and working hard to build it, in order to lay the foundation for the country's eternal stability.

Seventh, "The ultimate goal of the Three Principles of the People is to treat the social diseases caused by capitalism throughout the world, to build a new communist society with the common efforts of all mankind, and to complete a truly people-owned, people-governed, and people-enjoyed world of Great Harmony, that is, to create a world where there is no poverty, no scarcity, and no insecurity." One article is about the method of gradually implementing the Three Principles of the People by China, and one article is about the ultimate goal of the Three Principles of the People, which is to negatively treat the social diseases caused by capitalism throughout the world, and to positively create a "people-owned, people-governed, people-enjoyed" ideal world of Great Harmony. The problems that have arisen in capitalist society are numerous. The biggest point is the disparity between the rich and the poor. The poor have no food to eat, and the rich are extremely rich. The Three Principles of the People is the right medicine to cure all the social diseases of capitalism and achieve the goal of people-owned, people-governed, and people-enjoyed. This kind of great reform, which takes the world as its scope, requires the common efforts of all mankind. With the common efforts of all mankind, a communist society throughout the world, that is, the so-called world of Great Harmony, can be built. Therefore, the Three Principles of the People is true communism that enables everyone to have clothes to wear and food to eat, not the fake communism that generally loots houses, kills, and sets fires. (To be continued)

Qingpu

The Result of Loving Smoking and Gambling

Wu Xiangsheng, a farmer from Jiufang Bridge in the eighth district of the county, has three daughters, but he has been addicted to smoking and gambling since childhood and does not engage in proper work. Although his father repeatedly taught him, he still did not listen, so he was ordered to live separately. In less than a few years, he squandered all his family property. A few days ago, he failed to borrow money from relatives and returned home empty-handed. In the evening, taking advantage of people's unpreparedness, he hanged himself. When his wife noticed, he was already dead.

Jiading

A Demonic Person Misleads the Public and is Detained and Sent to the County Bureau

Three miles northeast of Lou Tang Town in the fifth district, there is a Cao'an Temple with an image of Emperor Yue inside. Dong Feiyan, from the former Lu Du Bridge Township, lived there to recuperate and slept in the same room with Zhong Asheng, the temple keeper, who was a tailor by trade. During the Lantern Festival in the lunar calendar, Zhong pretended to be in front of the statue of Emperor Yue, treading on the soil to form a pool. Immortal water was found in the pool. At the same time, he claimed that Emperor Yue had possessed him, talking nonsense, saying that the immortal water in the pool could cure all diseases. Those who asked for medical treatment had to have him stroke the affected area. The news spread, and foolish men and women were misled by it. Hundreds of people came from afar every day, and each person was charged 200 copper coins, which was managed by the temple director Zhu Guifang. Within ten days, the income reached hundreds of yuan. Pan Jixiang, the director of the Lou Tang Public Security Branch, in charge, believing that the person was a demon misleading the public, ordered the police to detain Zhong on the 12th. During the interrogation, Zhong still claimed to be Duke Yue. Pan sentenced him to 15 days of detention. Wu Nianqu and Zhang Zhenfei, who were of the same mind as Zhong, gathered a crowd of three to four hundred people by beating gongs and resisted. The group went to the Public Security Bureau and claimed that unless Zhong was released, they would take action. Director Pan, feeling that the police force was weak and to avoid causing trouble, did not refuse firmly. Jiang Linxiang, the brother-in-law of Fei Yan, provided bail for his release. After Zhong was released, the crowd placed Zhong in a sedan chair and carried him back to the temple on their shoulders, setting off firecrackers along the way, feeling very pleased. After returning to the temple, he continued to mislead the public and collect money as before. Director Pan telegraphed the situation to the County Public Security Bureau. Mei Buchun, the district chief of the fifth district in charge, also telegraphed the county government to stop it. On the 14th, Xue Bingyang, the director of the Public Security Bureau, sent four detectives to pretend to seek medical treatment and tried to lure Zhong to Lou Tang, then detained him and sent him to the bureau. It has been three days since then, and there has been no news of sending him to the county. All parties believe that this trend cannot be allowed to grow, and they are paying close attention to the handling of the Public Security Bureau. On the 15th, there were still more than 700 Buddhist women in the temple gathering to hold a Amitabha meeting, and there were still many people seeking immortal water.

Wuxi

Meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees of the County Chamber of Commerce

The County Chamber of Commerce of this county held its first joint meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees yesterday after the second re-election. Cai Jiansan presided over the meeting. (1) It was resolved that the monthly report and final accounts of the Chamber of Commerce should still be submitted to the meeting for reporting as before, and should be reviewed by the Supervisory Committee. In addition, it was decided that 2:00 PM on the 18th of each month would be the date for the regular meeting of the Supervisory Committee to emphasize accounting. (2) The reorganization of this session coincided with the decline of the business market. It should be earnestly presented to the local government offices and all tax collection agencies to understand the difficulties of the merchants and to maintain their business in the event of any incident, so as to stabilize business. As for the guilds of various industries, which are originally organizations of the same industry, as long as the same industry is at peace with each other, the organization is sound. It should also be requested that the Party and government agencies take into account that the merchant group is not comparable to a political organization. In the future, if there are any deficiencies in the procedures for the reporting of organizations by the guilds of various industries, or if the procedures are occasionally not in compliance, it seems appropriate to understand the original situation and avoid multiple criticisms, so as to maintain business and promote it. (3) The fence of the open space along the street of the Chamber of Commerce's East Gate collapsed. It is planned to plan and rebuild the city houses. It was decided that the Standing Committee would be in charge of contacting and handling the matter.

The Deputy Director of the Second Branch Bureau is Placed Under Custody and Dealt with According to Law 105

Liu Zhuomin, the deputy director of the Second Branch Bureau of Public Security, was dismissed by the provincial authorities for his poor handling of affairs, and Gao Chongshan, the deputy director of the First Branch Bureau, was appointed to fill the position. However, Liu Zhuomin refused to hand over the position. Liu's wife, Li Rongzhen, caused a great disturbance at the bureau, which turned into a theatrical drama in the officialdom. After the County Magistrate Yan ordered the Public Security Bureau to send armed police to take over, the matter was finally brought to an end. Yesterday (17th) afternoon at 2:00 PM, County Magistrate Yan ordered Deputy Director Gao to take over and ordered Xu Yi, the director of the guard stock, to go to the bureau to supervise the handover. Liu Zhuomin, knowing that he was at fault, handed over the seal and documents one by one. County Magistrate Yan, believing that Liu Zhuomin had left his post without authorization, refused to hand over the position, and embezzled more than 200 yuan of public funds, which violated the law and discipline, ordered Deputy Director Gao to place Liu under custody and transfer him to the General Bureau for transfer to the County Government for interrogation that evening.

The Collapsed Hall of the Buddha Crushed an Old Woman to Death 106

In Anji Village, Xi'an Bridge, Yangshu Garden, Sixteenth District, there is a Guanyin Temple. The temple is in disrepair for many years and the house is dilapidated. Recently, dozens of women gathered in the temple to chant the Seven Buddhas for seven days and seven nights. The general Buddhist women all lived and ate in the temple, and the sound of bells and Buddha's name never ceased day and night. The day before yesterday was the day of the completion of the Buddhist hall. Unexpectedly, at night, the loft suddenly collapsed, and the house collapsed, and all of them crushed an old woman to death and seriously injured two people.

Suzhou 107

Repaying the Principal and Paying Interest on the County Public Debt

Since the issuance of county public bonds, the principal and interest have been paid in installments every year. By last year, it should have been paid in full. However, due to financial difficulties, both the principal and interest have been postponed for repayment. The Bond Management Office held a meeting yesterday (17th) and resolved: (1) The extended interest silver of 14,950 yuan for the year of the Republic of China 22 will be distributed to the China and Communications Banks for distribution to bondholders. (2) The repayment of principal and interest of the fifth phase of bonds will start on April 9, totaling more than 149,000 yuan.

Higher Courts Add Branch Courts in Various Places 108

The Suzhou Higher Court, in accordance with the order of the Ministry to implement the three-trial and three-level system, has uniformly changed the county courts and district branch courts in various places into district courts and added more higher branch courts. President Lin has submitted the expenses for adding higher branch courts and the list of recommended names to the Ministry for approval. According to the plan, in addition to the first branch court in Qingjiangpu, the second branch court in the Shanghai Public Concession, the third branch court in the Shanghai French Concession, and the fourth branch court in Tongshan, the Zhenjiang District Court will be changed into the Higher Fifth Branch Court. The Zhenjiang District Court will be attached to the branch court. All second-instance cases in Xuhai Road will be handled by the Fourth Branch Court in Tongshan, and the second-instance cases in Jinling Road will be heard by the Fifth Branch Court in Zhenjiang.

A Clan Uncle Sells His Niece into Prostitution 109

Wang Jinxiu, a 17-year-old woman from Changzhou, lost her parents in her early years. Last spring, she was deceived by her clan uncle and brother to Suzhou, where she was sold to Gu Chen's Yaofeng Brothel at No. 6 Dexian Lane, outside of Changmen, to be a prostitute. Jinxiu was unwilling and tried to escape many times. When there were no customers, she was often beaten by the madam. Over the past year, she had been covered with wounds and her body was incomplete. The night before last (16th), she met a customer who was a police officer at a certain hotel. Unexpectedly, when it was time to sleep, two police officers slept together. Jinxiu was afraid and refused, shouting for help. Gu Chen was helpless and had to return the night fare, taking Jinxiu back and giving her a severe beating. The next day (17th), Jinxiu took the opportunity to deceive a gold ring from the ear of Gu Chen's niece, Yuanyuan, and escaped to the station to sell it, hoping to get money to buy a ticket to return home. The road police saw that she looked distraught and questioned her, knowing the truth, so they escorted her to the women's reformatory. Unexpectedly, Jinxiu was too badly injured. After arriving at the station, she vomited and diarrhea non-stop, and fell into a coma in bed. After being transferred to the county hospital, she was diagnosed with pneumonia and peritonitis, and there were serious injuries to her chest, back, lower abdomen. Her gallbladder and stomach were also severely injured, so she was hospitalized for treatment. At the same time, the madam Gu Chen was detained and sent to the Public Security Bureau. When Jinxiu first arrived at the hospital, she had recounted the suffering of the brothel and asked to rescue her three prostitutes in the same hospital.

Changshu

The Director of the Agricultural Education Center is Arrested and Imprisoned

The County Education Bureau convened the directors of various township agricultural education centers and social education institutions on the 14th to hold a social education meeting in the city. Zhou Mingjun, the director of the Fushan Agricultural Center, Guo Naizhen, the director of the Lao Wu City Agricultural Center, and Director Hou Jiren, etc., resided in the Huishang Hotel in the city. On the night of the 15th, Zhou and Guo had nothing to do to kill time, so they invited many people to gamble. The incident was discovered by the patrol team of the Public Security Bureau, which detained Zhou, Guo, and the teahouse staff together, and found prohibited items such as opium paste in their rooms. On the 16th, they were sent directly to the county judiciary. After Huang Cheng, the trial member, interrogated them, they were each sentenced to three months of imprisonment for smoking opium, and each was fined ten yuan for gambling. After the sentencing, they were immediately sent to the county detention center for custody. The agricultural education center's seals and other items were sent to the Education Bureau for receipt. The Education Bureau temporarily suspended Zhou and Guo and appointed the directors of each center to act as agents, pending the return of Ge Renyuan, the director of the Education Bureau, to Changzhou before making a decision.

Changzhou 110

Meningitis Spreads in Urban and Rural Areas

Due to the scarcity of rainfall and shallow rivers in Wuyi recently, meningitis has occurred in urban and rural areas, especially in the Qishu Yan area. If treatment is delayed, there is a danger to life. The Wujin Hospital has been extremely busy these days. Yesterday (16th), four more patients with this disease were sent to the hospital, one was Huang Fengying from Xinfeng Town, one was Qian Pingsheng from Zhoujia Lane, and two were girls of workers from the Qishu Yan Power Plant. All of them had acute meningitis, and the disease was extremely severe. After the doctors treated them, it is not yet known whether they are in danger. At present, various institutions and organizations are discussing ways to prevent the spread.

Hangzhou

Zhejiang Education Department Seeks the True Image of King Goujian of Yue

In order to commend the local culture, the Zhejiang Education Department is now planning to compile and print small biographies of ancient worthies and martyrs to serve as extracurricular reading for children in order to promote national aspirations. Recently, a small biography of King Goujian of Yue has been compiled in simple language. The cover of the book is planned to be copied with the image of King Yue. However, at the time, no original copy was available. It was decided to solicit information from various places. If there are stone carvings or records in ancient books, rubbings, or family-owned portraits, etc., which are confirmed to be authentic and not fabricated temporarily, they may be properly sent to the fourth section of the department before April 15. After being adopted and photographed, a generous reward will be given, and the original will be returned safely.

Thieves Rob Two Families in Tangxiu Township

In the Tangli Third Society area of Tangxiu Township, Sixth District of Shaoxing County, there is a resident named Zhu Zhangfu, who is doing business in Shanghai and is quite wealthy. He returned to the village a few days ago. Knowing that he had brought wealth home, more than a dozen thieves gathered together last night (16th) and broke down the gate, swarming in. Local News

Nine Aircraft from the Aviation School Flew to Shanghai Yesterday Afternoon 114

Participating in the Naming Ceremony of the Tianchu Aircraft Today

The naming ceremony of the Tianchu fighter plane and the handover ceremony of the Yuehui, Yuewen, and Tianchu Deputy aircraft will be held at 2:00 PM today at the Hongqiao Airport. The Aviation Administration sent nine aircraft to Shanghai yesterday to participate in the performance. The Central Government has also designated senior officials to come to Shanghai specifically to represent the acceptance. At that time, there will be a grand event on Hongqiao Road.

Venue Setup 115

The venue is located inside Hongqiao Airport. Li Dachao of the Municipal Government, together with Fang Zhicheng of Tianchu Factory and Tang Chengzong of the Du Mansion, went yesterday to complete the setup. The main stage is set in front of the newly built hangar, with a portrait of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen and the flags of the Party and the Nation hung above. In front of the stage, white banners with black characters reading "Naming Ceremony of Tianchu Main and Deputy Aircraft" and "Presentation Ceremony of Du Yuesheng's Gifted Aircraft to Sun" are displayed. Seven police squads dispatched by the Public Security Bureau are guarding the venue, while soldiers from the Security Office are stationed outside the venue. At the entrance, fourteen inspectors from the Public Security Bureau are collecting admission tickets. The setup is quite thorough.

Traffic Routes

The Organizing Committee of the Tianchu Aircraft Naming Ceremony, considering that today is Sunday and many people will be visiting, which is bound to cause congestion, has dispatched more police officers from the Public Security Bureau to direct traffic along Hongqiao Road. To avoid congestion, the routes are designated as one-way. The outbound route is from Xujiahui, via Hongqiao Road, directly to the airport. The return route is via Paifang Road and Luobiegen Road. To facilitate the audience, the Municipal Public Works Bureau has ordered the China General Omnibus Company to add several buses at Xujiahui starting at 12:00 noon today to transport the audience. The fare is 20 cents per person, which takes you directly to Hongqiao Airport.

Ceremony Program

(1) The presidium of the ceremony includes Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Wu Yunshu, Du Yuesheng, Shi Liangcai, Lin Wojiang, Wang Xiaolai, Yu Qiaqing, and Master of Ceremonies Yu Pu; (2) For the ascension ceremony, Mrs. Wu Tiecheng for the Tianchu aircraft, Mrs. Wu Yunshu for the Tianchu Deputy aircraft, Mrs. Du Yuesheng for the Yuehui aircraft, and Mrs. Zhang Xiaolin for the Yuewen aircraft, will perform the bottle-smashing ceremony. Originally, champagne was used, but Mayor Wu suggested changing to Shaoxing wine to promote domestic goods.

Xu Peigen, Director of the Aviation Administration, in order to encourage the public to promote aviation to save the country, specially dispatched the squadron of the Administration, flying nine aircraft donated to the government by various circles in Shanghai, including the "Shanghai City," "Shanghai Business," "Shanghai Industry," "Shanghai School," "Shanghai Boy Scout," "Lianglu," "Ningbo," and "Zhejiang Save-the-Nation" trainer planes, from Hangzhou to Shanghai at 2:00 PM yesterday, landing at Hongqiao Airport. Those who came to Shanghai on the planes included Mao Bangchu, Principal of the Aviation School, Gao Zhihang, Captain, and instructors Liu Chao, Zhang Yuanbei, An Jiaju, Nie Jingyu, Wang Boyue, Xu Jindian, Huang Guanghan, Liu Cui Gang, Hao Hongzao, and more than ten others.

Technical Performance

The nine aircraft that arrived in Shanghai from Hangzhou yesterday will perform as a team today. The Aviation Administration also ordered Gao Zhihang, captain of the first squadron, to perform various combat maneuvers. The young aviator Sun Tonggang will also participate in the performance after receiving the aircraft donated by Du Yuesheng. There will be various thrilling maneuvers to feast the eyes of the audience.

Overseas Chinese in Mexico Urgently Request Assistance as Anti-Chinese Sentiment Intensifies 116

The Overseas Chinese Federation recently received a letter from the Overseas Chinese Chamber of Commerce in Mexico, which reads, "Regarding the anti-Chinese party named 'Pro-Race Patriotic Association' in Ensenada, Baja California, Mexico, whose primary goal is to expel Overseas Chinese. They have recently been distributing leaflets and making announcements everywhere, exclusively boycotting Chinese people, demanding the expulsion of our people. On the evenings of January 25th and 26th, speeches were made in theaters, all with insulting and malicious words. For several days, they paraded, shouting the slogan of expelling Overseas Chinese, and using cloths to write words such as 'Expel the Chinese' and 'Strictly Enforce Boycott.' In this situation, our people dare not look up. On March 4th, the same thing happened again, with a surging momentum, treating Overseas Chinese as enemies. On the morning of the 5th, several leaders directed party members, with a party badge sewn on their left sleeves, to guard each Chinese-owned store with two people, prohibiting Mexicans from entering the stores to buy anything. The local police have no authority to intervene. Complaints to local officials are ignored. Several letters and telegrams have been sent to our country's minister in Mexico, requesting serious negotiations with the Mexican government to stop the boycott and the dangerous actions of the rioters. It has been several days, and we have not seen instructions from Minister Huang. All Overseas Chinese are panicked and in imminent danger. We have no choice but to send this letter to your office to present the dangerous situation, hoping that you will consider the meaning of being of the same race, find a way to rescue us, and also request that it be published in newspapers, and forwarded to our country's embassy and consulate in Mexico, so that they can know the urgency of our situation and find a way to rescue us with all their strength, so that we can avoid being harmed by the anti-Chinese party. We would be very fortunate. Sincerely, the entire Overseas Chinese population of Ensenada, Baja California, Mexico, salutes you. February 6, 23rd year."

Chiang is satisfied with the draft constitution.

Yesterday, Mr. Sun received a group of reporters at his residence on Columbia Road, discussing the meeting with Chiang Kai-shek in Jiangxi. His remarks are recorded below:

Chiang has no objection to the draft constitution.

Sun said first, "This time, I went to Jiangxi to meet with Chiang Kai-shek to seek his opinion on the draft constitution and to discuss the affairs of the Economic Commission. The financial issues were discussed directly between Minister Kong and Chiang, so I am not familiar with the details. As for diplomatic issues, they fall within the scope of Director Wang, and we did not discuss them. Chairman Chiang is satisfied with the initial draft of the constitution. I am still studying it and have no specific opinions, but I hope that the whole country, from top to bottom, will refer to the national conditions and express their opinions as much as possible, paying attention to practicality, so that a perfect constitution can be compiled, which can lay the foundation for national affairs."

The Central Government hopes that Hu will travel to Nanjing.

Sun continued, "Mr. Hu Zhantang has a long history in the Party and is one of the Standing Committee Members of the Central Political Council. All comrades in the Central Government respect his opinions very much and hope that he can travel to Nanjing as soon as possible to take joint responsibility. Last year, the Central Government repeatedly sent personnel to the south to welcome Hu to the north, but it did not become a reality. Therefore, whether Mr. Hu is willing to go to Nanjing or not is his personal freedom, and others should not force him. The rumors that I sent a letter to Hu urging him are not true."

Great progress in bandit suppression military operations. 119

"Regarding the bandit suppression military operations in Jiangxi Province, since Chairman Chiang Kai-shek stationed himself to supervise the suppression, all the bandits have been defeated and dispersed, and many occupied areas have been recovered. Chiang has recently been very determined to encircle and suppress the bandits in Jiangxi, and plans not to return to Nanjing temporarily before the bandit suppression military operations are concluded."

The Economic Commission will hold a general meeting. 120

Sun also said, "The funding of the National Economic Commission is currently quite difficult. Minister Kong has discussed this with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. The source of funds is from the US cotton and wheat loans. However, due to the abundant domestic production of US cotton and wheat, sales are slow, so we have no choice but to negotiate with the United States to reduce the amount of the loan, from US$50 million to US$20 million. It is expected that the US will eventually agree. However, US$20 million is only 60 million yuan in national currency. After deducting 20 million yuan for transportation and handling fees, the remaining amount is only 40 million yuan. Therefore, the various construction plans originally set by the Economic Commission will not be able to proceed in an orderly manner, or else it will be necessary to find other ways to raise funds. The standing committee members of the Economic Commission have decided to convene a general meeting of all committee members within two weeks, before Committee Member Song (Ziwen) goes to the Northwest for inspection, to discuss the allocation and remedial measures."

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce again requests instructions on how to deal with fellow traders who do not join the association. 128

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce previously received reports from various trade associations stating that fellow traders resisted joining the association, the spirit of the association was dissipated, and the associations jointly requested the government to formulate measures to sanction those who did not join the association in order to facilitate economic control. The original text has been recorded in previous newspapers. It is learned that the association received instructions from the Ministry of Industry yesterday, which did not approve the formulation of implementation measures, and therefore presented a rebuttal based on reason. The original texts of the approval and presentation are recorded separately below. Approval from the Ministry of Industry: The presentation has been received. Article 7 of the Trade Association Law states that companies and firms in the same trade should be members of the Trade Association. Therefore, those in the same trade in the same area should naturally join the association, fulfill the obligations of members, and abide by the articles of association. However, there are no provisions for sanctions in this law. Only the association itself can, in accordance with Article 1 and Article 4, Section 7 of the same law, stipulate punishments for violations of the articles of association in the articles of association. The law does not grant the Ministry the power to formulate implementation measures, and the Ministry is not in a position to formulate them without authorization. The information presented is hereby acknowledged. This approval. The Chamber of Commerce resubmits: (Omitted above) Regarding the so-called traders in the same area who do not join the association, the Ministry of Industry stated that only the association itself can, in accordance with Article 1 and Article 4, Section 7 of the Trade Association Law, stipulate punishments for violations of the articles of association. After further research, there are still many doubts. Although traders in the same area have the obligation to join the association as members in accordance with the law, the acquisition of membership qualifications is only possible after the trader himself applies to join the association. Now, let's compare the articles of association of the association to the school rules. The articles of association can only punish members, just as the school rules can only punish students. Traders in the same area should join the association in accordance with the law, which is the same as the situation in countries that implement a compulsory education system, where children of school age should be ordered to attend school in accordance with the law. If there are those who resist not joining at this time, only the administrative authorities can punish them, and it does not seem possible to entrust the school to punish students who have not entered the school in accordance with the school rules. Moreover, the above situation is still theoretical, and according to the facts, it is even more absolutely unfeasible. The most effective method for commercial organizations to punish members who violate the rules is to suspend the rights that members should enjoy, and in the most serious cases, to expel them. The rest are not within the power of the association. If those who resist not joining the association are punished by the above methods, they have not joined the association in the first place, and originally did not expect to enjoy the rights of members, and expulsion would also have nothing to expel. To speak of punishment in this regard is actually the same as no punishment. If the association forwards this order, the various associations will still have no way to act, and they will inevitably come to question it. It is appropriate to submit another request to the Ministry for clear instructions on the method, so that there is something to follow. It is in the public interest.

Jianghai Customs Issued Three Announcements Yesterday 129

Tang Hai'an, Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, and Borel de, Tax Commissioner, in order to comply with the government's order, must collect the full amount of import duties for foreign rice transported from Fujian, which were previously reduced by half, and that ships traveling around the world that have not been loaded with cargo should be charged half the tonnage tax of ordinary ships, and that the office will be closed on the anniversary of the martyrdom of the seventy-two martyrs, issued three announcements, Nos. 1345, 6, and 7, yesterday. The following is a separate record: (1) It has been found that foreign rice transported to Shanghai from Guangdong, Guangxi, and Fujian must be taxed for import duties starting from December 16 of last year, as stated in Announcement No. 1330. Now, the government has ordered that, starting from March 15 of this year, foreign rice transported to Fujian should be taxed at half the current import duty rate. However, if it is re-transported from Fujian to other provinces, it should be taxed at the full import duty rate, and the half that was previously reduced in Fujian should be made up at the port of arrival. All merchants should be informed of this. This announcement is hereby issued. (2) It has been ordered by the government that ships traveling around the world that have not been loaded with cargo should be charged half the tonnage tax of ordinary ships. In addition to complying with this order, all merchants should be informed. This announcement is hereby issued. (3) It has been found that the 29th of this month is the anniversary of the martyrdom of the seventy-two martyrs. The government has stipulated that there will be a one-day holiday. This customs office will be closed on that day in compliance. All merchants should be informed of this. This announcement is hereby issued.
