North China Hurricane: Three Steamships Encounter Danger 132

The North China Sea has been hit by hurricanes for days. Within the past three days, merchant ships encountering danger and sustaining damage include the Hexing, Lianxing, and Pingji. They have suffered from damaged machinery, severe peril, or destroyed cargo. Our reporter has investigated in detail and recorded the situations as follows:

Hexing: The Hexing ship of the Zhaoxing Company had just been repaired in the Lushun shipyard, with more than 300 iron plates replaced throughout the ship. After completion, it sailed to Shanghai, and then on the 13th, it loaded miscellaneous grains and foreign cloth to Yantai, Longkou, and Dalian Bay from Shanghai. It sailed from Wusong in the morning, and on the 15th, it reached the Black Water Ocean. The ship was immediately hit by a hurricane. The ship fought desperately against the storm in the raging waves. Having entered the hurricane circle, it was impossible to stop. It could only sail with all its strength. The ship was repeatedly in danger. The deck and cabin surface were often rolled in by waves. The cargo holds were filled with seawater, and much of the cargo was soaked and damaged. After ten hours of crisis, it managed to escape the hurricane circle. The ship is now approaching Longkou, but the cargo in each hold has been severely damaged. The amount of loss will only be verified after unloading at the port.

Lianxing: The Lianxing ship of the Zhaoxing Company was loaded with more than 1,200 tons of soybean oil, peanuts, cement, etc. It sailed from Tianjin via Yantai and Weihaiwei to Shanghai. It encountered a hurricane as soon as it sailed out of Weihaiwei.

For the sake of navigation safety, the ship urgently sailed to the Rongcheng Bay Strait and anchored for two days to avoid the strong wind. On the morning of the 15th, it received a weather report from the observatory stating that the storm had passed. The Lianxing then set sail from Rongcheng directly to Shanghai. At 8 a.m., the ship arrived north of Sheshan, at 1.37 degrees east longitude and 33 degrees north latitude. Suddenly, the hurricane struck again, with the wind coming from the west-northwest. At this time, the Lianxing had no way to avoid it and could not turn the ship around. The magnitude of the wind and waves was alarming. A wave hit, the waves surged over the signal bridge, and hit the ship from the side. From the shipowner down to the crew, all the Lianxing personnel were mobilized for the rescue work. They risked going forward, because if they faced the wind, the ship would be broken. If they retreated, they would be immediately overturned. The gale and giant waves came like overturning mountains and seas. The ship rolled to thirty degrees on the sea surface. The cabin surface was no longer safe to stand on. There were more than 20 passengers in the ship. After this unprecedented crisis, they all resigned themselves to certain death. The hurricane lasted twelve hours, from 8 a.m. to 8 p.m. They were driven from 33 degrees north latitude to 35 degrees north latitude. Thanks to the joint efforts of the shipowner and crew, they managed to escape the hurricane circle. However, the shipowner's outdoor structures were destroyed by the waves, and many of the oil drums in the large cabin were broken due to the hull’s constant rolling. It was not until the evening before last that they safely arrived in Shanghai. It was truly a fortunate escape. Yesterday, the shipowner reported to the company, which sent personnel to inspect the ship. The damaged parts need to be repaired slightly.

Pingji: The Pingji ship of the Zhidong Company in this port sailed from Shanghai to Yantai, Tianjin, etc. The ship was loaded with miscellaneous grains. The ship also encountered a hurricane when it reached the Shandong Sea. The ship was battered by wind and waves for more than ten hours. Because the ship braved the waves forward, fighting against the storm, the machinery engine was damaged. The ship then sailed from the Yellow Sea to the Rongcheng Bay Strait and anchored for repairs. When the Lianxing sailed out and encountered the wind, the Pingji was having its machinery broken by the strong winds and waves. The ship is still under repair.

Special News from the Shipping Industry 133

Transporting Saltpeter to Fujian to Blast Mountains: The Fujian Provincial Government is constructing an upstream highway to facilitate bandit suppression, troop movement, and traffic development. The work is already underway. However, the upstream areas of Fujian are mountainous, and to build the highway, mountains must be blasted through to create a level road. The provincial government has decided to blast the mountains obstructing the highway. It has sent Zhou Zhongsan of the Fuzhou Saltpeter and Sulfur Bureau to Shanghai to purchase 5,000 kilograms of saltpeter for blasting mountain roads. He will be ordered to transport it to Fujian for use as soon as possible. To transport this saltpeter, the Fujian Provincial Government sent a telegram to the Sanbei Company in Shanghai yesterday, instructing Commissioner Zhou to contact the company to arrange for loading and shipping. It is planned to ship it to Fujian tomorrow to be received by the Highway Construction Department.

The National Goods Conference Reduces Fees, but River Steamer Prices Rise, Causing Panic in the National Goods Industry. The cost of goods such as galoshes, thermos bottles, and enamelware is less than 100 yuan per box, but the freight costs more than 100 yuan, causing national goods to stop being loaded into Sichuan from February 10th for 40 days. It is distressing to see inferior goods taking the opportunity to enter the market. Because the new agreement on increased river steamer fees is about to be extended for six months, Yu Qiaqing of the Sanbei Company, as a shipping merchant, should also consider society. Various industries expressed that they could not agree with such a large increase in national goods freight. Yesterday, Mr. Yu invited representatives from various national goods industries and representatives from the seven river steamer companies to a meeting at the Shipping Club. The two sides directly discussed the inappropriately increased prices and reduced them one by one according to the cost of the goods, dividing them into different levels to avoid driving away customers and helping inferior goods to be sold in Sichuan. The two sides are currently negotiating the new freight rates, and all prices are expected to be revised by the end of this month.

Xing Zhigang Petitions for the Construction of a Public Justice Wharf 135

Xing Zhigang, a representative of the western shipping merchants in Pudong, submitted a petition to the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Works yesterday, requesting that it assist in the approval and, together with the Bureaus of Finance and Public Utilities, allocate funds to construct a public and just wharf to maintain commerce and facilitate transportation. It stated, "The Wanyu, Gongyi, Yongsheng, Dongjiadu, and South Guild Hall wharves in the South City have long been the gathering places for ships from various towns and townships in Pudong West, Fengxian, Nanhui, and Chuansha counties, and the busiest ports for the loading and unloading of goods for various businesses along the inner and outer roads of the South City. Now, the Wanyu Wharf has been suddenly abolished due to the construction of a rented warehouse. Not only can the ships and passengers originally docked at the port not load and unload, but the newly built municipal houses on the street have few visitors. Commerce has suddenly changed and plummeted. Therefore, the issue of the existence or abolition of a port directly affects the prosperity or decline of commerce, and indirectly affects the income of the municipal treasury and land taxes. The matter is extremely important and significant. The Bureau has been aware of this and submitted it to the 244th Municipal Council meeting for discussion. It was decided to designate the three Bureaus of Public Works, Finance, and Public Utilities to plan the addition of a public wharf near the Wanyu Wharf, draw up plans, and estimate the price. In October of last year, the Municipal Government issued Directive No. 7756, stating, 'All the submitted documents are noted. Regarding the addition of a public wharf to the Gongyi Wharf site, since the price has been assessed and according to the opinion of the Finance Bureau, the total should be within 10,000 yuan. Save expenses and allocate funds when the land value tax is received.' The review is considered appropriate and should be handled as proposed. Now that the land value tax has been levied for some time, and funds are available, the construction of the wharf is essential to maintain transportation in the four townships and the transportation of commerce. There should be no delay. Therefore, it is requested that the Bureau approve the decision, and together with the Bureaus of Finance and Public Utilities, allocate funds to construct a public and just wharf to maintain the transportation of thousands of ships and people from the townships and develop the business of various businesses in the South City."

Four Chinese Telegraph Code Characters Added 137

壋, 琱, 砟, 郾

Effective April 1st

The Ministry of Communications believes that although the domestic telegraph code is still perfect, there are still omissions in the application of the code. To facilitate users, four characters have been added: (1) The code for 壋 is 8250; (2) The code for 琱 is 8874; (3) The code for 砟 is 8895; (4) The code for 郾 is 9251. The new codes will be effective from April 1st. The Ministry ordered the various telegraph offices in this port to comply yesterday.

Gu Jigao Lectures on the Silver Problem 138

The China Industrial and Commercial Management Association of this port, in view of the fact that the problem of rising silver prices is closely related to our country's finances and national economy, specially invited Gu Jigao, an economics expert, to lecture on the significance of this problem and the countermeasures that our country should take at the United General Association yesterday. People from industrial and commercial circles went to listen to the lecture in large numbers. More than 50 people, including Li Zhaohuan, Cao Yunxiang, and Pan Yangyao, attended. The speech was recorded by Bingxun Stenography, and the gist of the speech was that the United States' raising of silver prices is unfavorable to our government finances, agriculture, industry, commerce, finance, and international trade. Although it may be slightly beneficial to the repayment of foreign debts, the gains do not outweigh the losses. As for the countermeasures, there are temporary and permanent solutions. The former is not discussed because the government has already made considerable preparations. The permanent countermeasures can be divided into three types: (1) Change to a managed silver standard so that the purchasing power of silver is controlled by us to facilitate domestic production; (2) Change to a gold standard. Because world prices have already risen, our country's prices will also rise after the change to gold, and production will develop; (3) Improve production technology, management, and monetary reform should be carried out simultaneously.

Health Bureau Inspects Meat Entering the City 140

The Municipal Health Bureau believes that meat is a daily necessity and is closely related to the health of consumers. It is a matter that should be inspected and supervised by the health administration. The pre- and post-slaughter inspections of pork, beef, and mutton sold in the city have been carried out for many years. However, although the regulations for inspecting meat entering the city were promulgated by the Municipal Government in October 1910, meat merchants have repeatedly requested a delay due to misunderstandings. On March 15, 1933, the Municipal Government issued an order stating that, in accordance with the order of the Executive Yuan, this inspection is aimed at eliminating diseased meat entering the city and maintaining public health. Before the Ministry of Industry and Commerce has formulated measures for the domestic sales inspection of goods, it should be temporarily approved. The Health Bureau, together with the Social Affairs, Finance, and Public Security Bureaus, consulted and approved the implementation of the inspection of meat entering the city from April 1st. The Health Bureau appointed doctors to inspect meat entering the city at the main land and water entrances, such as Shanghai North Station, South Station, Wusong, Xin Jing, and South Huangpu. They also ordered the inspectors to provide convenience to the transporters within the scope of the fixed regulations. Therefore, all pickled and fresh meat sold in the city has been inspected. The inspection fee is only 10 cents per 50 kilograms. Once the scientific inspection proves that the meat is unhygienic due to being from livestock with epidemic diseases, it will be confiscated according to regulations.

Maid Helps Master Chase Thief, Snatches Gun and Gives it to Master Who Wounds Thief 146

Detective Liu Shaotian is Also Shot by Mistake

Wounded Thief Sent to Hospital Awaiting Recovery Before Interrogation

Deng Shaonong, a 36-year-old Cantonese man, lives at 7 Baoxing Lane, North Henan Road, in the Public Concession. He is a small owner of the Pudong Xin Sanlin Company and also a comprador at the Dongyang Wharf. His wife, Ms. Shen, is 33 years old, and his concubine, Ms. Zheng, is 28 years old. Both have children and the family is quite wealthy. Unexpectedly, it was coveted by bandits. At about 9:40 a.m. yesterday, when Deng Shaonong had not yet gotten up, four bandits wearing black cloth jackets and trousers suddenly appeared outside the back door. Three of the bandits had pistols, and one bandit stepped forward to knock on the door. At that time, only the hired maid, Jiang Ma, was sweeping and cleaning downstairs. Hearing the knock, she

went to open the door and asked the bandits what was the matter. The bandits claimed to be from Pudong and had important business to see Mr. Deng. The maid thought it was a regular visitor and did not suspect anything. She allowed them to enter. Unexpectedly, the bandits ordered one bandit to guard the back door, one bandit to watch Jiang Ma, and two bandits rushed upstairs and broke into Deng's bedroom. They woke the victim and frightened him into silence. Deng, caught off guard, had to let them search and rob. After about half an hour, the bandits began to flee with the stolen goods. Deng Shaonong, seeing this, quickly put on his clothes and chased out, and chased after them with the maid. He shouted "Catch the robbers!" The bandits, realizing things were not good, desperately fled north. Unexpectedly, one of the bandits, in a panic, accidentally stumbled and fell to the ground, and the pistol he was carrying fell out. At this time, the maid Jiang Ma had caught up. Seeing the opportunity, she stepped forward to hold down the bandit, grabbed the gun on the ground, and handed it to Deng Shaonong. Deng then fired a shot at the bandit, hitting him in the abdomen. Blood flowed freely. At the same time, the nearby patrol officers arrived and arrested the wounded bandit and took him to the police station. According to the bandit, his name is Wang Axiao, from Jiangbei, 33 years old. When asked further, he was unable to speak clearly due to his injuries. He was taken to the hospital by car for treatment and will be interrogated after he recovers. The remaining bandits escaped and the police station has sent detectives to pursue them. However, when the victim Deng Shaonong shot at the bandits, Detective Liu Shaotian of the police station happened to be sipping tea upstairs in a nearby teahouse. Hearing the alarm, Liu quickly chased out of the teahouse. Seeing the bandits running away, he planned to draw his gun to pursue and arrest them. Unexpectedly, the victim saw him and thought he was an accomplice of the bandits. He also shot Liu in the leg. As a result, Detective Liu was accidentally wounded and fell to the ground. Fortunately, the patrol officers realized the mistake and rushed to report it to the Hongkou Police Station, which sent a car to rush Detective Liu to the hospital for treatment. Fortunately, the injuries were minor and there was no major problem. The amount of losses is difficult to calculate, but the victim claims that it is a very large amount.

The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities Facilitates Transportation in South Shanghai 148

Public Buses to Start Operating Next Month

The Central News Agency reporter heard that the South Shanghai public buses would start operating next month and visited Xu Peihuang, Director of the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities. Director Xu was out on official business and was received by Zhang Dengyi, Chief of the Fourth Section of the Bureau and Director of the South Shanghai Public Bus Management Office. He was informed of the following details:

Preparations 149

According to Mr. Zhang, the Bureau, in view of the importance of transportation in South Shanghai, and at a time when the municipal treasury was extremely tight, negotiated a credit loan with foreign merchants, which was agreed upon by both parties and approved by the superiors. Preparations were then started. A total of 16 vehicles have been ordered from foreign merchants and will first run on the Longhua to West Gate and Round City routes. The factory site is located at the old site of the former South Shanghai Public Bus Company, which is also to save expenses.

Opening Date 150

Currently, all internal staff have been appointed, and drivers will soon be recruited. Most vehicles are nearly completed, and the Xieqiao factory site has also been re-arranged. The bus stops remain in their original locations, but the station signs have been replaced with clearer and more noticeable ones. Therefore, the opening ceremony is hoped to be held on April 1st. However, if the project requires a slight delay, the service should definitely be operational by April 10th.

Consideration for Travelers 151

The purpose of our bureau in launching the Shanghai-Nanhui public bus service is to serve the public. The route is more profitable, while the Longhua-Ximen line only sees better business around the Qingming Festival each year, with very little activity during other times. Therefore, this line is expected to be loss-making. However, given that private buses have been setting high prices and taking advantage of rainy days since the suspension of the Shanghai-Nanhui public bus service, causing great inconvenience to travelers, our bureau cannot effectively regulate them. Therefore, to consider the needs of travelers, our bureau has had to sacrifice and restore traffic on this route.

Vehicle Prices 152

There are currently sixteen vehicles, each with a load capacity of three and a half tons, which is one ton more than those operated by commercial entities. The cost per vehicle is approximately eight thousand two hundred yuan. The upper part of the vehicle body is painted in ivory color, the lower part in green, and the waistline is decorated with black and white squares.

Ministry of Railways Plans Cold Storage Facilities on Various Lines 155

Decision Made to Proceed in Three Phases

Two Lines Listed in the First Phase

The Ministry of Railways believes that because China's railways lack cold storage transportation facilities, fresh fruits, vegetables, fish, eggs, etc., produced along the various railway lines cannot be sold in other regions to regulate supply and demand. This has led to the decline of the agricultural economy and hindered the development of railway operations. To address the issue of regulating the people's food supply and supporting agricultural production, and at the same time open up a new avenue for railway business, a plan has been proposed to establish a cold storage system across the national railways. However, due to the large construction costs, which are difficult to raise in the short term, it has been decided to proceed in three phases. The full text of the construction plan is excerpted below:

Construction in Three Phases The national railway cold storage project will be carried out in three phases. The first phase of construction includes: (1) cold storage warehouses in Shanghai and Nanjing; (2) an ice station in Hangzhou; (3) ten refrigerated cars. The total cost is approximately 560,000 yuan. The second phase of construction includes: (1) cold storage warehouses in Tianjin and Qingdao; (2) ice stations in Beijing, Jinan, Xuzhou, and Haizhou; (3) twenty-two refrigerated cars. The total cost is approximately 680,000 yuan. The third phase of construction includes: (1) cold storage warehouses in Guangzhou and Hankou; (2) an ice station in Wuchang; (3) twelve refrigerated cars. The total cost is approximately 550,000 yuan. The total construction cost for the three phases is over 1.8 million yuan. As for the construction steps, Shanghai is a distribution center for fresh goods. The output of fresh goods along the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo lines is extremely large. Moreover, it is close to the capital, making supervision and management easier. It is appropriate to implement the project there first to serve as a model. Therefore, it is listed in the first phase and completed first. The second phase is an expansion period. To promote the joint transportation of fresh goods, it is necessary to continue the project on connected railway lines. Furthermore, the capital's ferry service is already open, making north-south transportation more convenient. Therefore, the cold storage facilities on the Tianjin-Pukou, Jiaoji, and Longhai lines are included in the second phase. Two years later, the Yuehan Railway will also be completed, forming a continuous line with the Beijing-Hankou Railway, which is an important north-south route. Therefore, it is included in the third phase for completion. The first-phase plan includes cold storage warehouses in Shanghai and Nanjing, an ice station in Hangzhou, and ten refrigerated cars. The detailed plan is as follows: (1) The construction site for the Shanghai cold storage warehouse is selected in the empty space within the Maigen Road freight station. The site is located southwest of the Maigen station, west of the Suzhou River. Goods can be unloaded directly from cargo ships at the warehouse. To the south is a railway track connecting to the Maigen Road station, and further south is Kangji Road, which provides access to the city center via Jinling Road, Xinzha Road, or Xinmin Road. Therefore, the location is very convenient for railway, waterway, and land transportation. The cold storage warehouse occupies a length of sixty-five meters and a width of forty meters. However, the initial construction only occupies half of the land. The warehouse will be doubled in size in the future when business develops. The original track in front of the warehouse will be replaced with new sleepers and ballast to accommodate the parking of trains. The warehouse has a total of five floors. The first floor has a large storage room for handling goods transportation, a workers' rest area, and an ice-making area and machine room. Below is the cold storage cellar. The second and third floors are the main storage areas, each divided into four cold rooms for the separate storage of fresh goods. The fourth and fifth floors are rental warehouses, each divided into four cold rooms. The rooms are separated by round iron bars and wire mesh to create small storage spaces of four and six square meters for merchants to rent. The machine room is connected to the warehouse and located in the northeast of the warehouse. The lower floor includes a machine room, equipment room, repair room, and materials storage area. The upper floor houses offices and a transformer room. The machine room is equipped with two argon refrigeration units, capable of providing sufficient capacity for the entire cold storage warehouse and ice-making area to produce 15.52 tons of ice per day. (2) The Nanjing cold storage warehouse is selected on the empty land next to the freight warehouse at the Xiaguan Station as the construction base. The warehouse is twenty-five meters long and twenty meters wide, covering an area of ​​500 square meters. There are two railway tracks to the northwest of the site. It is planned to set up a unloading platform there in the future, which will be very convenient for parking freight cars. There is a main road to Tokyo that leads directly to the city center. To save on start-up costs, only three floors will be built first. The various facilities are similar to those in the Shanghai warehouse. (3) The Hangzhou ice station will build an ice-making room next to the station, equipped with two argon refrigeration units for ice-making. (4) The ten refrigerated cars are forty-ton, eight-wheeled cars. The outer length of the car body is 11.2 feet, the width is 2.8 feet, and the height is 4.2 feet, with a load capacity of 10 metric tons. Each car is equipped with two iron ice boxes at both ends, each storing about 600 kilograms of crushed ice.

Profitable Operation After the completion of the first phase of construction, the estimated operating income is: (1) Shanghai warehouse: about 150,000 yuan; (2) Nanjing warehouse: about 90,000 yuan; (3) Hangzhou ice station: about 30,000 yuan, totaling 280,000 yuan. After deducting operating expenses, machine and warehouse depreciation, and investment interest of more than 220,000 yuan, the surplus can be more than 50,000 yuan. However, the tonnage of fresh goods transported will definitely be more than the current estimated number after the cold storage is established. Therefore, the actual profit should increase.

Melting National Currency into Silver Ingots 156

Although Legally Not Punishable

The Judge Sternly Reprimanded in Court

Since the Ministry of Finance officially issued an order to abolish silver smelters in Shanghai, most people who engaged in the silver smelting industry have been unemployed or have changed careers. A person from Shaoxing named Qi Chufa also belonged to the silver smelting industry. Recently, he set up the "Duan Tai" business at No. 20 Yixing Lane, Qipu Road, and No. 41 Tiantong Road, specializing in the business of melting raw silver. The Municipal Public Security Bureau learned of this and believed that Qi and others were melting national currency into silver ingots, violating the order of the Ministry of Finance. Therefore, they, together with the detectives from the Concession Police, arrested Qi Chufa and six others, and confiscated 879 double cents, 26 silver ingots, 62 pounds of broken silver, and four molds. They were all sent to the First Special Court. In addition to applying for transfer of the case, the Municipal Public Security Bureau also reported to the Ministry of Finance for review. Later, Zhan Jifeng, the legal advisor of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, presented the order from the Ministry of Finance during the previous court hearing, requesting a review. However, Jiang Baolian, the lawyer of the Public Works Department, argued that there were no explicit legal provisions for such cases, making it difficult to prosecute. Jiang Yiping, the attorney representing Qi and others, stated that Qi and others had not violated the law and should be released. The court ordered a review and filed the case. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu Tingqi delivered the following verdict at the Eighth Criminal Court: "Qi Chufa, Qian Guoxun, Chen Jinshan, and Shen Yushu's act of privately smelting silver ingots against the order is highly inappropriate. In addition to being sternly reprimanded in court, the molds should be immediately destroyed, and Qi Chufa should be responsible for requesting the Central Mint to recast the silver ingots into silver coins in accordance with Article 1 of the Silver Standard Coinage Ordinance. Zhou Huilin and Tong Dasheng are innocent and released."

Under the Cruel Authority of a Fierce Woman, the Adopted Daughter Dared Not Speak 157

Using a Feather Duster as a Weapon

The Adopted Daughter's Injuries Proven to Be Real

—Verdict: Fine of Ten Yuan, Girl Returned to Maternal Uncle—

A woman named Chen Fan, from Changzhou, residing at No. 20 Wusong Road, has been mistreating her eight-year-old adopted daughter, Ge Gengnan, constantly beating her and causing injuries all over her body. At around 10:00 AM the day before yesterday, she again used a feather duster to strike the girl's hands and legs severely. Gengnan, in pain, ran into the street crying, where she was spotted by an elderly woman from Suzhou, Li Lushi, who lived nearby. Li took her home, learned the details of what happened, and gave the girl lunch out of pity. Later, she planned to send her back home with gentle words of advice, but the girl said that she would be beaten to death if she went back and pleaded for help. Therefore, Li reported the situation to a Chinese detective on patrol nearby. Detective Wu Deyi took her to the Hongkou Patrol Room, reported to the head detective, and sent the girl to Tongren Hospital, where the injuries were confirmed. He ordered Detective Wu to secretly arrest Chen Fan and send her, along with a feather duster, to the detention center. Yesterday morning, she was sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special Court. Wang Yaotang, the lawyer of the Public Works Department, recounted the events and claimed that the defendant said in the patrol room that she beat Gengnan because she stole money. He presented the injury report from the feather duster for examination. Li Lushi testified about what happened, but the girl, Gengnan, was afraid of the defendant and did not speak clearly. The court ordered Chen Fan to be taken out of the courtroom before asking the girl, "Did your mother (i.e., the defendant) beat my hands and legs with a feather duster for taking a silver coin to buy sesame cakes and candies?" Chen Fan confessed that Gengnan had been adopted from her mother, Zhao Guiying, two years ago and that the girl had stolen silver coins three times, so she beat her. She added that Gengnan's maternal uncle, Zhao Yonggen, was in court and could be asked. Zhao testified that he was from Wuxi and that Gengnan was indeed his niece. His sister, Guiying, was being detained in court for opium use after being arrested by the Hongkou Patrol Room. He asked that the girl be handed over to him to return to their hometown to be raised by his mother, to avoid being violently beaten by Chen Fan. The court ordered the judicial police to bring the girl's mother, Guiying (i.e., Ge Zhao), from the detention center to the courtroom. After verifying that Gengnan was indeed her daughter, she said that the defendant should not have beaten the girl so badly and asked that she be handed over to her brother, Yonggen, to be taken back to their hometown. Upon hearing this, Chen Fan became furious and pointed at Ge Zhao, saying, "If you want to punish me, I will tell the truth and confess that Gengnan was sold to me as a daughter for fifty yuan. At that time, she said that if the girl was not good to you, you could beat her as you pleased. Please, Your Honor, be aware!" Ge Zhao admitted to receiving forty yuan previously and giving the girl to the defendant as her daughter, but she did not tell her to beat her severely and requested that the girl be taken back to their hometown by her younger brother, Yonggen, etc. Judge Xiao Xiefei sentenced Chen Fan to a fine of ten yuan and ordered the girl, Gengnan, to be taken by her maternal uncle, Zhao Yonggen.

The Murderer in the Brothel Bloodbath Was the Patron 158

Abandoning the Old for the New Led to the Poisonous Act

A Strict Investigation Is Underway to Find the Murder Weapon

The Madams and Pimps Were Released

On the morning of the twelfth of this month, at 8:00 AM, a tragic murder occurred at the brothel located at No. 15 Hengmao Lane, Bassen Bridge, Mintini Yin Road, in the French Concession. The prostitute Wang Guixiang and her patron, Mr. Wang, were both brutally attacked. The prostitute Wang died on the spot, while Mr. Wang suffered severe injuries and was taken to Guangci Hospital for treatment. Afterwards, Chief Inspector Jin Jiulin of the French Patrol Room, along with Head Detectives Zhang Ziying and Qian Yumin, and Deputy Detectives Jiang Changwen, Zhou Yaoting, Zhou Buguang, Yang Yilong, and others, conducted a thorough investigation. They learned that Mr. Wang's real name was Wang Yuhe, also known as Runjiu, from Shandong Province, aged forty-eight, residing at No. 227 Xuzhen Road, Xujiahui. The deceased prostitute had borrowed three hundred yuan from Wang Yuhe in June of last year, and they had made a promise to stay together. However, recently, the deceased had a change of heart and planned to go to Wuhu with another patron, a fishmonger. Wang Yuhe learned of this and demanded repayment of the debt. However, the deceased spoke disrespectfully, angering Wang. Overwhelmed with grief and resentment, Wang conceived a murderous plan, willing to die with the deceased. It is said that there was a seven-inch-long pair of scissors hidden in the drawer of the prostitute Wang's room. Since the bloodbath, the scissors have disappeared. Therefore, Chief Inspector Jin is currently ordering a strict investigation to find the murder weapon. The madams and pimps arrested in connection with the case have been cleared of any involvement and released.

American Private Tour Group Arrives in Shanghai 160

An American tour group of four hundred and seventeen male and female members of the 1934 South Seas tour arrived in Shanghai yesterday afternoon aboard the SS President Lellin. According to the group's leader, Mr. Brooks, they plan to leave Shanghai at 9:00 AM tomorrow morning, first going to Qinhuangdao, then to Beijing and Tianjin, to inspect the famous historical sites of the ancient capital. They will then sail to Yokohama, Japan, stay for about three days, and then travel to Honolulu before returning to the United States.

Puyi Society and Household Improvement Association Hosts Women's Circles in the City Yesterday 161

Huang Renzhi Speaks on the Importance of Family Education

Yesterday afternoon, the Shanghai YMCA began holding a members' recreation exhibition at Dadongmen, featuring photography, the Bible, ancient scriptures, ancient and modern coins, stamps, calligraphy and painting, cultural anecdotes, flowers and birds, antiques, puzzles, and homemade cloth. At the same time, a eyebrow painting competition was held. Chinese and Western people went to visit, which was quite lively. The exhibition continues today and tomorrow. Tomorrow afternoon, a recreation festival and performance will be held. The association's Household Improvement Association also hosted women's circles in the city yesterday to discuss household improvement matters. During the session, the general secretary of the association, Zhu Wang Wanqing, reported, stating briefly: "If you want the country to be sound, you must start with the family first. As the saying goes, 'When the family is in order, the state will be well governed; when the state is well governed, the world will be at peace.' However, today, many people lack a deep understanding of the family, which has led to social unrest. The family is the foundation of society and the country. I hope that you will work hard to promote the improvement of the family." Next, Huang Renzhi spoke, briefly saying, "The family is the first society that children encounter. A good family creates good children. Therefore, if you want a good society, you must first educate children, especially starting with family education. Therefore, the quality of the family is related to the strength of the country and cannot be ignored."

Water Outage Dispute at Jingye Lane, Caishi Road, French Concession 163

Citizens' Branch Holds Emergency Meeting

According to Huadong News Agency, Yu Yifeng of Chenghua Company, the owner of Jingye Lane at the intersection of Caishi Road and Kangdi Road in the French Concession, hired lawyer Ni Guangzu in March of last year to represent him in claiming to the residents that the water bills were too high and therefore rent needed to be increased. The original rent for each shikumen building was 28 yuan, and for each storefront was 30 yuan, and all were increased by 40%. The residents had no choice but to agree to the rent increase. However, on the 6th of this month, the residents of the lane suddenly received a letter from the French Water and Electricity Company, instructing them to sign a water contract with the company within two days, or the water supply would be cut off and stopped. At the same time, they also received a notice from the landlord that because the water bill was too high, the tenants would be responsible for it. After receiving the letters, the residents felt that they had already increased the rent last year because the landlord claimed the water bill was too high, and it had been a year. The landlord did not understand the residents' difficulties and continued to oppress them. Moreover, at a time when the market was sluggish, all sectors were trying to reduce rent, so they were unwilling to sign a contract with the water and electricity company voluntarily. Because the residents did not sign the contract by the deadline, the company sent people to cut off the water line of the lane yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM. The residents of the lane had no choice but to elect seven people, including Chen Yazhang, Shi Caizhang, Yuan Chengji, Lu Quanyuan, Yan Jingbai, Xia Xinyuan, and Shen Jinsheng, as representatives to request the Second Special District Municipal Employee Branch to uphold justice and send a letter to the Taxpayers' Association for assistance. The Fifth Branch of the Second Special District City Federation, after receiving the report of the water outage, was afraid of causing a major dispute, so it immediately issued a notice summoning all the committee members of the lane to hold an emergency meeting at the assembly hall of Li Yuan Lane, Lan Weiai Road, at 8:00 PM last night to discuss countermeasures.

Public Concession Board Revises Tent Tax 164

Shops Still Claim Tax Amount Too High

Citizen Association Issues Notice to Postpone License Application

Shops in the French Concession, which previously paid a tent tax of five jiao per shop annually, had the tax revised last year by the French Public Concession Board. The new tax was calculated based on the area occupied by the shop, at a rate per English foot. This increased the tax to approximately three to five yuan per shop annually, causing opposition from various shops. They requested the Citizen Association of each district to petition the Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the French Concession to discuss remedial measures. The meeting resolved to appoint Vice Chairman Mr. Cheng Zhusun to repeatedly negotiate a solution with the French authorities. Mr. Cheng reported to the association members the outcome of his negotiations: a tax of one yuan per shop annually, with a fixed license fee of five jiao. For double-fronted shops, an additional one yuan would be added per front, with similar increments for additional fronts. However, this was only a verbal agreement, and the French authorities continued to collect taxes according to the increased method, based on English feet. Therefore, the dispute was not fundamentally resolved. The Citizen Associations continued to request the Taxpayers' Association to discuss countermeasures and sent a letter to the French Public Concession Board requesting a reduction in the tax. After Mr. Cheng's repeated efforts to negotiate, the French authorities decided to revise the tax fee and agreed to publish it in writing in the Chinese Gazette of the French Public Concession Board. Unexpectedly, the list of various taxes published in the January 1934 Gazette showed that the fixed tent license fee was seven jiao per paper, and the tax fee was one yuan and five jiao per shop annually, or three yuan for a double shop, with similar increments for additional fronts. This was still inconsistent with the original negotiated amount. As the weather has recently become gradually hotter, shops are in the process of applying for licenses. The French Public Concession Board is still calculating fees based on English feet and collecting fees according to the newly defined method. The minimum cost per shop is two yuan and two jiao annually (including the fixed tax), which is an increase of seven jiao compared to the originally agreed fixed tax of five jiao and tax fee of one yuan. Furthermore, the calculation per front is one yuan and five jiao, an increase of five jiao. Thus, the license fee has not been reduced. Many who are unaware of the true situation are paying fees calculated based on English feet, and they have repeatedly inquired with the Citizen Associations about why the fees have not been reduced and why they are being collected according to the newly defined revised method, requesting further negotiations. Upon receiving these reports, the Citizen Associations have forwarded the information to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the French Concession, based on the figures published in the French Public Concession Board's Gazette, to continue negotiations with the French authorities for a reduction. They have also notified all shops to temporarily postpone applying for tent licenses until a definitive solution is reached, after which they can apply for licenses and pay taxes.

Second Special Court Burns Confiscated Drugs and Gambling Equipment 168

The Jiangsu Shanghai Second Special District Local Court, from October to the end of December last year, confiscated opium, morphine, red pills, heroin, smoking paraphernalia, and gambling equipment seized by the police. President Ying Shi and Chief Prosecutor Chen Beisan decided to hold the ninth incineration ceremony at 2:00 PM yesterday in the open space east of the court. Prior notice was given to the Ministry of Judicial Administration and the Third Branch Court of Jiangsu Higher Court, and letters were sent to military, political, legal, police, and various organizations in Shanghai, including the Bar Association, the Anti-Drug Association, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, inviting representatives to supervise the event. This was briefly reported previously. Yesterday, on the scheduled date, the court's general affairs section hired workers to set up reed mat sheds and seats in the open space east of the court. The head of the confiscated goods section ordered court staff in the morning to move all the drugs and gambling equipment to the site and arrange them in rows on both sides. At 2:00 PM, representatives from the Ministry of Judicial Administration, Shanghai Local Court President Shen Xiqing, and the Third Branch Court representative Tang Zaili, as well as representatives from various organizations, arrived at the site. President Ying, Chief Chen, and Chief Clerk Li Ping welcomed them and escorted them to their seats. Court clerks Chen Shengyan and Xu Chenghuang then ordered court staff to move each item of drugs to the front of the representatives' seats for inspection, sealing, and weighing before piling them in the center of the site. Firewood was placed around the pile, and kerosene was poured on it before setting it alight. After the drugs were burned, the gambling equipment was burned. This incineration included 1,363 cases of drugs, totaling 37.5 catties of opium, plus 28 packages of 7 pounds, plus 32 taels; 59 boxes of opium paste; 563 opium bubbles; 85,037 red pills, plus 17 packages, 2 pounds; 2 packages of morphine; 19 packages of heroin; 308 opium pipes; 5,765 red pill guns; and countless smoking paraphernalia and equipment for making red pills. There were 1,345 cases of gambling equipment, including 649 lottery tickets, 28 lottery books, 10 lottery manuals, 9 pairs of dominoes, 45 mahjong sets, 14 decks of playing cards, 70 dice, and countless abacuses, pencils, stamps, printing cylinders, and miscellaneous items. The ceremony concluded at 4:30 PM, and the representatives departed.

Page 14

Telephone Bureau Notifies Users Not to Transfer Telephone Service to Others 170

The Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation notifies users as follows:

Regarding the matter of some of our users who, finding they no longer need their installed telephone, do not report it for removal but arbitrarily transfer it to others for use. Some may do this occasionally due to a lack of understanding of the regulations, but it is feared that others are taking advantage of this for personal gain. This violates the regulations. Any violations that are discovered will be punished according to Article 18 of the regulations. The bureau cannot condone such actions, nor can it allow them to continue. To prevent abuses and facilitate both parties, please consult the regulations printed in the telephone directory and follow the proper procedures. The original user only needs to report the removal, which only requires the effort of sending a notification letter. Please do not arbitrarily transfer the service, which will only cause unnecessary losses to the person taking over the service. This notice is hereby issued for your information and attention.

Two Young Men Attempt Suicide in Yangtze Hotel 171

One Dies... One in Critical Condition

At around 7:00 PM the night before last, two young men suddenly arrived at the Yangtze Hotel on Hankou Road and requested lodging. The hotel provided them with Room 70. One of the men was Guo Xiwen, age 22, and the other was Xu Kangtai, age 22, both from Chongming. They paid six yuan for the room at the time. At around 10:00 PM that night, they closed the door and went to sleep. Unexpectedly, at around 9:00 AM yesterday morning, the tea server on the floor heard moaning sounds from the room and became suspicious. He immediately opened the door and saw the two men writhing in bed, their faces pale. A small amount of opium was found beside their pillows. It was discovered that they had taken poison. The server quickly reported to the accounting office, who notified the Lao Zha Police Station. Officers were dispatched to rush the two men to Renji Hospital for treatment. Unfortunately, Guo Xiwen died en route due to severe poisoning. His body was sent to the coroner's office for examination. Xu Kangtai regained consciousness briefly after being treated at the hospital. He claimed that they had each swallowed one yuan's worth of raw opium. They were both in the Nanhua goods business and had been driven to this by economic pressure. He soon lapsed back into unconsciousness. It is difficult to say whether his life can be saved.

Honors for Officer Xu of the Water Patrol Team 178

—Merchants and Residents Unanimously Appeal for Recognition—

The second squadron of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's water patrol team is stationed between the Xinzha Bridge and Hengfeng Road in Zhabei, with jurisdiction extending from the Waibaidu Bridge to the Zhaojiadu Zhongshan Bridge. However, the river surface in this area is narrow, with sails moving back and forth like shuttles, and the riverbanks are densely packed with sampans. Especially during the winter low tide season, traffic congestion often occurs. The area is strategically important and notoriously difficult to patrol. Since Officer Xu Chizhi took charge of the team, he has worked hard to rectify the situation, paying particular attention to water traffic and maritime security. As a result, there have been no kidnapping or theft cases in the more than a year since he took office, and water traffic has been well-organized, without any congestion. Therefore, merchants and residents on both banks, such as the Rice Association, Fuxin Flour Mill, Inland River Shipping Association, Siming Shipping Association, and Coal and Stone Transport Association, are all very pleased. They admire Officer Xu and have jointly appealed to the relevant authorities for recognition. They also intend to express their appreciation in some other way.

Establishment of the China Self-Supplying Insulated Bottle Factory 179

Ministry of Industry Approves Patent Rights

During the year of national products, domestic manufacturers are striving to improve themselves, competing to create new inventions to contribute to society. This is a positive sign of scientific progress and national development. It is recently learned that financiers and industrialists Xu Tingfang and Xu Rongfang, brothers, invented a self-supplying insulated bottle in June of last year. Its design is similar to European and American coffee pots, and it can maintain heat for up to forty-eight hours, making it more convenient than ordinary thermos bottles. It comes in various sizes and specifications, and the decorations and accessories are exquisite, beautiful, and purely domestic. Xu Rongfang applied for a patent to the Ministry of Industry, which was approved by the Ministry of Industry's Technology Review Committee on October 12 of last year. The patent was granted for five years, and the committee noted that the bottle was very practical and that the glass tube in the lower part of the bottle was unique to this insulated bottle. It is learned that Mr. Xu has raised a large amount of capital and is preparing to set up a factory to manufacture the bottles. It is expected that the product will be a sensation when it is launched, and its convenience will be appreciated.

The World's Smallest Radio: The Kaidian Pocket Radio is the smallest radio invented in the United States. It is called "KADETTE" and weighs only two pounds. It can be carried anywhere and connected to AC or DC power (110 volts). It does not need a ground wire or antenna because it is already installed in the machine. The body is made of real bakelite in various colors, which is durable and does not change. Its reception performance is not weaker than ordinary machines. Programs from Nanjing and Japan can be received clearly and loudly. A speaker can be installed and connected by wire, with a distance of 15 to 50 feet. The sound is as loud as a large machine. The machine is currently sold by Fuxing Wireless Electrical Material Store, No. 374 Beijing Road, Shanghai.

Reading Q&A 187

Further Discussion on

Steps in Literary Study

Writing and Others (3)

The above has presented three propositions for studying literature, and we have already discussed (1) What is the literature we need? and (2) How to read literary works. Today, we will continue the discussion: (3) How to create? We hope readers will also refer to the several essays on literature that we have published previously. Editor

(3) How to create? Humans have a desire to express themselves, and the desire to create for those who study literature is a natural requirement.

However, the general public has two opposing and equally erroneous views regarding creation. These two views are most likely to hinder the development of creative power and must be corrected immediately.

1. Fear of Creation. Some people see creation as very mysterious, as something that ordinary people cannot hope for. This is not right. The reason we see it this way is because we see creation as purely a technical issue, the exclusive domain of scholars and literati who have studied for many years and possess literary cultivation. Technique is necessary, but technique is not the main condition for creation; the main thing is content. Technique will improve as your creative life progresses. A child who has been beaten will "cry," a person who has been wronged will "sigh," and dockworkers will hum "Hey ho!" when they are carrying goods. These simple emotions are the elements of literature. We are living a difficult life, and our daily life is a very good creation, just waiting for us to honestly describe it in words. If you are an apprentice, why can't you write about your daily life of being scolded and beaten and pouring out slop buckets and washing pipe ash? If you are a machine worker, why can't you shout out the pain you suffer from the factory owner, the foreman, and the machine? If you were born into a declining farming family, you can write about the sadness of decline; if you are unemployed or out of school, you can write about the panic and desolation of unemployment or being out of school. Moreover, humans are thinking animals, and in such a life, we always have our own hopes, we have the future of our lives, and these are also the content of creation. We already have a rich life, so why should we be afraid of creation? What is so mysterious about creation? Is it because scholars and literati write about "azure skies," and we can't change it to "blue skies"?

2. Chaotic Creation. Mr. Shen Congwen, a now famous literary figure and professor—this name should be familiar to everyone—once had this idea about how to write a novel: that writing a novel only requires random thoughts and random writing. Is this right? We cannot assume it is right just because he is a professor and a literary figure; it is not right. Such random thinking and random writing can only be done by literati who treat creation as entertainment and by literary craftsmen who treat creation as a wealthy person's enjoyment. We should not do this. We want to think, but we are not fantasizing. Our thinking must be based on the society in which we live and closely tied to our own lives. We want to write, but not aimless moaning; our writing is to cry out the suffering of life and expose the evils of society. Therefore, our creation is not for the sake of creation, but for the sake of social life. Not only must our attitude toward creation be serious, but especially our lives must be serious. That is to say, we must not be manipulated by fate and float along with the world, but we need to combine our lives with all the forces that promote society. Only with a real life can there be creation; random thinking and random writing will never succeed. Don't look at others, just look at Mr. Shen Congwen himself, who has written so many books. Since he ascended to the throne of professor, enjoying a leisurely life and not competing with the world, what else has he been able to write!

In short, the prerequisite for creation is a rich life. We must neither "fear" nor "be chaotic." Our main move is simply to observe society and experience life. With this move, we have completed the preliminary and fundamental work of our creation.

Then, we will talk about the process of composing a creation.

The backbone of a novel or a drama is the story. We are not talking about poetry here because poetry, except for narrative poems and epics, is poetry without a story; it is just a moment of high emotional impact, like the dockworker mentioned earlier who naturally hums the tune of "Hey ho...Hey ho" when working.) When writing, the first thing we must ask ourselves is, in this complex social phenomenon, in this tedious life, which fragment should we extract as the subject of our creation? If this question is resolved, we will organize the extracted fragment through our minds and construct a simple and orderly story. This includes recognizing where the focus of the story should be, that is, what is the central point we are expressing, and how the protagonist should appear in this story. If this step is completed, then we can unhesitatingly use the words we can use to write the story as it is. After writing it well, of course, it cannot be considered a work yet. Then, we can carefully revise it in terms of language and structure. Where we feel the description is insufficient, we must strengthen it; where we feel the description is redundant, we must delete it. The standard of our descriptive technique is concise and clear, that is, to see whether the point or character we want to express in the story has been fully expressed, and whether it can give people a sense of pleasure at a glance when reading. We do not necessarily need those gorgeous words and playful sentences. Moreover, to say it again, we must never focus on those words first when we write.

Looking at the above, regarding how to study literature, at least it can give readers a concept, right? Now, there are two more subordinate questions that we might as well bring up and discuss.

Some readers have written to ask: (1) When studying literature, should one read literary creations first or theory first? (2) Does studying literature require reading social sciences? The answers to these two questions are: (1) Originally, creation and theory are interconnected and should be advanced together. Theory is the guideline for creation, and creation is the backbone of theory. But now all learning has become specialized, and creators and theorists are already working hard on their respective paths, although theorists still cannot but read creations, and creators cannot but understand the preliminary theory, but they each have their own biases. Therefore, to determine this question, readers must first decide whether they are studying literary theory or creation. However, for beginners, we believe it is best to read creations first, because the principles of theory are ultimately derived from creation. (2) In today's society, not only those who study literature, but everyone should have some basic knowledge of social sciences. However, if your life does not allow you to have enough time to read, then at least you must read two books on "dialectical materialism," because this can help you to recognize and analyze society, and even understand the direction in which society is moving and how you should live. For a literary person, in addition to the experience of actual life, this is also a necessary condition for studying literature.

International Basketball

Women's Championship Triangular Showdown: Chinese Team Lost to England Last Night 191

Defeated by a three-point margin, 25-28

China, the United States, and England to Replay Finals Next Week

The International Basketball Tournament held two women's matches last night at 8 o'clock. The men's championship was decided last Wednesday, with the American team winning with two wins out of two games. Although the Chinese team was eliminated from the men's championship, there was still hope in the women's competition. The Chinese women had previously defeated the United States in their first match and then defeated the Federation in the second. In last night's match, the first game was between the United States and the Federation, and the second game was between China and England. If China had won last night, the championship would have been theirs. Unexpectedly, the Chinese team was defeated by a three-point margin, resulting in a triangular standoff between China, England, and the United States, each with two wins and one loss. A replay between the three countries is needed to determine the championship. It was expected that the United States would defeat the Federation last night. However, the defeat of the Chinese team by England was beyond the expectations of most people. The details of the two matches are recorded below:

United States Defeats the Federation

—26 to 18—

The United States defeated the Federation with ease. In the first quarter, White of the United States opened the scoring, and the Federation struggled for a long time before Marto scored a goal. Shortly after, White scored again, and Bausack of the United States added another goal and two free throws. At the end of the first quarter, the United States led 10-2.

At the beginning of the second quarter, Marto of the Federation scored under the basket, raising his hand successfully. Then, Boram scored a free throw and four consecutive points. Marto then scored another single-handed shot. At this point, the Federation took the lead 11-10, turning defeat into victory. The United States seemed to be caught off guard in the second quarter.

However, the Federation's momentum felt weak. At the beginning of the third quarter, relying on the momentum from the previous quarter, Leswana scored a goal first. However, White of the United States then scored two consecutive goals and continued to dominate, leaving the Federation at a loss. In the fourth quarter, the Federation struggled hard, but to no avail. As a result, they were defeated by the United States 26-18.

China Loses to England

—28 to 25—

As soon as the battle began, after a minute of close combat, Parkhill of England opened the scoring, and V. Princes scored two free throws. Shortly after, Chen Rongming, with the assistance of Yang Sen, was able to retaliate, and then scored a free throw. Yang Sen also raised his hand successfully, and Chen Jucai also scored from an out-of-bounds throw. Chen Rongming scored another point from a free throw, and V. Princes also scored a free throw. At the end of the first quarter, the Chinese team led 8-5.

At the beginning of the second quarter, Princes scored first again. Chen Rongming missed many free throws, while Chen Jucai, with the assistance of Liao Zhuyuan, was able to shoot successfully. After that, the enemy scored four consecutive points, and the Chinese team was defeated by one point. Shortly after, Chen Rongming scored two more points, but V. Princes of the enemy team returned two points. The Chinese team was again suppressed by one point. In this situation of sudden advances and retreats, the first half ended with a score of 12-13, with the Chinese team suffering a small defeat by one point.

After the break, V. Princes scored under the basket, and Parkhill gained an unexpected long shot. Yang Sen rushed to the basket and tossed it in, adding two points, but the enemy also added two points. Yang Sen scored another goal, but was still one point behind the English team. Then, Chen Rongming scored a free throw, resulting in a tie of 19-19. After that, the English team scored three consecutive points, while the Chinese team scored a goal by Yang Sen and a free throw by Chen Rongming, resulting in a tie of 22-22. The third quarter ended.

The final quarter was a matter of life and death for both sides. The Chinese team missed many good opportunities, and the English team scored two points, putting the Chinese team in danger. Then, Chen Jucai called out Pan Meng, who scored a goal as soon as he entered the field. However, the enemy team became even more ferocious. In the end, Chen Rongming scored a free throw, resulting in a final score of 25-28. The Chinese team failed by a three-point margin. Observing the four quarters of the match, England committed many fouls. However, Chen Rongming and Yang Sen rarely made their free throws. Donghua Defeats Youyou One to Zero in the Last Quarter Hour 193

Both Sides Defend Tenaciously, Unable to Determine Victory

Wan Xianghua's One Shot Seals the Victory

—A Scene from the Western League Division A Match—

In the Western League Division A soccer match between Donghua and Youyou, the two teams met for the second time yesterday at the Chinese Baseball Field. As a result, Donghua defeated Youyou 1-0, avenging their previous惨败 at Yiyuan. The game was clear and harmonious, and both sides played with extreme caution in both offense and defense. It was not until the last quarter hour that Jiang Shanjing was injured and had to leave the field, and Donghua took the opportunity to score, sealing the victory with a score of 1-0. Only two or three thousand people watched the game.

Equally Matched: Yesterday's match between Donghua and Youyou was truly a case of evenly matched teams, with comparable strength. In addition, both sides played harmoniously, with no violent actions. Therefore, the tension of the game was greatly reduced, and both sides adopted a strict defensive strategy. The game progressed at a constant pace, neither hurried nor relaxed. One could say it was interesting, or one could say it was ordinary.

Two Crises: Donghua kicked off, Wu Shouheng blew the whistle, and with the wind at their backs, they went straight for Youyou. Dai and Li, the two forwards, advanced steadily, but Youyou defended strongly. Chen Jiaqiu, who was reassigned to defense, did not fail in his duty. Although Donghua had many attacks, they were unsuccessful. In the 25th minute, Wan Xianghua skillfully sent a ball from the left corner, which landed right in front of the goal. Xiao Dai saw that it was a good opportunity and took a shot, but Tang Yongchun caught it squarely, and the ball flew into the air. A gust of south wind blew it behind the goal, which was also a surprise. Then, Li Yichen's shot, which could have scored, was withdrawn due to Zhou Guangzhong's offside. These were the notable events of the first half.

Slight Change in the Situation: In the second half, the two sides switched positions, and Youyou had the wind at their backs, which changed the situation. Sun Jinshun was reassigned to center forward, and Youyou also sent their three armies to advance on Donghua. Although Liang Shutang had many opportunities, his headers and kicks were inaccurate and ineffective. The cooperation between Zhong and Xi also often fell short. Donghua returned the favor, with Wan Xianghua being the most active. An Lesheng's weakness made Xiao Wan look much better. With a kick to the right, Jia Youliang could have received it and scored, but suddenly his foot did not extend and he fell. As a result of the siege, the score remained zero-zero.

Final Outcome: With only fifteen minutes remaining in the game, Youyou's defensive line suddenly collapsed. Jiang Shanjing, a key player, suffered a hamstring injury and had to withdraw. Then, Xiao Wan's charge and An Lesheng's misstep led to them冲进 the goal together with the ball. Xiao Tang could only sigh at his failure, and the stalemate was broken. Youyou's counterattack was weakened, and it was also difficult for Donghua to score again. The game ended with this one-to-zero score.

Local News

City Education Bureau Issues Order Explaining Names of Private Nursing Schools, 205

and Procedures for Establishing Student Level Standards

Shanghai City Education Bureau issued an order to private nursing schools stating: The bureau had previously found that there were no set regulations regarding the handling of private nursing school names, student levels, and establishment procedures. We had already submitted a request to the Ministry of Education for review and instruction. Now, we have received Directive No. 2328, which states: "Received and noted. Instructions are hereby issued separately as follows: (1) The terms 'senior nursing vocational school' and 'nursing' can be used interchangeably with 'nurse.' (2) Senior nursing or nurse vocational schools must not offer junior-level programs. Those enrolling elementary school graduates should have a five-year graduation requirement. (3) Private school regulations must be followed. (4) The length of study for senior nurse vocational schools is set at three years. Those enrolling elementary school graduates should have a five-year program. The curriculum should refer to the Ministry's outline of subjects and time allocation for vocational schools. The detailed teaching syllabus is being compiled by the Ministry. Please be informed."

This order is hereby issued to instruct the schools to comply accordingly. This order is given.

Attached is the original document from the Shanghai City Education Bureau to the Ministry of Education:

We have found that many hospitals and midwifery schools in the city also operate nursing schools. There are no initial regulations regarding the names of these nursing schools, student levels, and establishment procedures, making it difficult to operate. We hereby submit the following points for instruction: (1) Article 35, Section 4 of the Vocational School Regulations stipulates that senior vocational schools regarding household matters can offer courses in sewing, embroidery, nursing, and midwifery. We have found that private nursing schools in this city and Zhejiang Province are named "nurse," and we are unsure whether this can be equated with the term "nursing" in the regulations, or if it needs to be corrected. This is the first point. (2) According to the Vocational School Regulations, nursing schools should be at the high school level, enrolling junior high school graduates. However, in reality, most nursing school students are elementary school graduates or junior high school dropouts, and their graduation level is equivalent to junior high school. Therefore, private midwifery schools in this city often accept nursing school graduates. The reason for this is that very few junior high school graduates enroll in nursing schools, so they have to lower the requirements to accept elementary school graduates and junior high school dropouts in order to maintain operations. To adapt to the actual situation, can we now implement a flexible approach and allow the establishment of junior nursing schools in addition to senior nursing schools? This is the second point. (3) Regarding the procedures for these nursing schools to apply for establishment, can we temporarily refer to the regulations for establishing midwifery schools in addition to following the revised private school regulations, before receiving and implementing instructions from your ministry? This is the third point. (4) How many years should be the duration of study for nursing school students, what kind of courses should be taught, and how should internships be conducted? This is the fourth point. The following four points are all important issues for establishing nursing schools. We hereby submit this document to your ministry for review and instruction.

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

Children, Hurry and Strive 207

— Da Zhai

Japanese rickshaw pullers all read newspapers. When they are stopped on the street without any business, you often see them holding newspapers and reading them. This is because Japanese rickshaw pullers are all elementary school graduates, so they can understand what they read. In Japan, elementary school education is called compulsory education. If a child reaches school age and does not attend school, their parents will be punished. Therefore, everyone is literate, and there are no "illiterates." There are more newspapers than in our country, and more people read newspapers than in our country. The circulation of newspapers is many times higher than the daily circulation of various newspapers in our country. Looking back at our country, how many "illiterates" are there? Have you ever seen a rickshaw puller reading a newspaper? This is all because elementary school education is not developed. We only know how to hate the Japanese for being aggressive, but we must understand that their education is better than ours, which is why the country is so strong!

According to the 20th's newspaper report, the number of out-of-school children in Jiangsu Province accounts for 86 percent, approximately 4 million. Such a large number of out-of-school children is alarming. If Jiangsu is like this, what about other provinces? Judging from this, it is such a great blessing to be able to carry a schoolbag and go to school every day, thanks to the strength of one's father and brothers! If one does not strive to study hard, is that not being self-defeating?

As the saying goes, "Children are the masters of China in the future." The responsibility is very heavy, so this year is called "Children's Year." It is a pity that so many out-of-school children cannot be helped for the time being. I hope that all the children who are enrolled in school will become good students, so that our country will have hope in the future.

More than thirty years ago, Japan won the war against Russia, not crediting it to the army, but to the elementary school teachers, because the elementary school teachers cultivated good elementary school students nationwide, which resulted in the good outcome of winning against Russia. This shows that elementary school students have a great relationship with the country. Gu Tinglin said, "The rise and fall of a nation is the responsibility of every man." I will put it another way: "The rise and fall of a nation is the responsibility of every child." Out-of-school children have already lost their chance to study, and children in school should study even harder. The country is in such distress, children, hurry up and strive, hurry up and strive.

Lincoln 208

— Guo Pinjuan

Children, have you seen the name "Lincoln"? He was the sixteenth president of the United States.

His family was very poor, so when he was little he lived with his parents in a log cabin. Lincoln's bed was just a pile of dry leaves. But he didn't think it was hard, and was happy all day long.

He only went to school for one year, but he loved books and was willing to study hard.

He was very kind to people, and his friends loved him very much.

Later he became a lawyer, and the people of the United States respected and loved him very much. They elected him as the president of the United States. Lincoln then liberated the most painful black slaves in America, which was a great contribution to humanity.

He died in 1865, about seventy years ago.

Children, do you also respect and love Lincoln? You should take him as a model!
