Does the Sun Move? 211

— Bo Zhen

"Brother Cheng, I have a question that I am very doubtful about and want to ask you now. It is something I usually see and hear. Will you allow me to ask?" Shi'er was an eleven or twelve-year-old child, and his face showed hope that his brother would allow him.

Standing next to him was a child a little older than him, who was his brother—Cheng'er—who, hearing his younger brother asking him, said, "Shi'er, if you have any questions, ask me. Don't keep them in your heart and be afraid to ask, but I'm afraid I won't be able to answer questions that are too difficult."

Shi'er, hearing that his brother allowed him to ask, began to ask.

"Brother Cheng, every morning when I get up, I see a blood-red sun in the east, gradually rising from the east, and in the afternoon, gradually sinking into the west. Judging from this, the sun can move. But I also heard people say, 'The sun does not move. The sun's rising from the east and sinking into the west is because the earth is rotating.' Brother Cheng! Does the sun move after all? Since the earth rotates, then wouldn't we humans and everything else fall down?"

Cheng'er, because he was very familiar with this natural phenomenon, said very fluently.

"Shi'er, the stars in the sky that do not move are called fixed stars, and the stars that revolve around the fixed stars are called planets, and the stars that revolve around the planets are called satellites. The sun is one of the fixed stars, so it does not move. The earth is one of the planets and revolves around the sun, and it rotates from west to east, endlessly, so we see the sun rising from the east and sinking into the west every day. The earth does rotate. However, we humans and everything else will definitely not fall down, because there is a very strong attraction inside the earth, which is called gravity, which attracts humans and everything else, but humans can still move freely."

Shi'er was very grateful for his brother's words, because his brother had given him a new kind of knowledge.

How to Spend Spring 212

— Sha Yi

Winter took away his son—snow, and the goddess of spring, with both hands outstretched, began to descend to the world. My clever children! Do you already have plans for spring?

You must know that spring is the most beautiful season, so don't miss it. You must fully appreciate it. Children! If you haven't made any plans yet, choose from the following:

(1) Travel Collect a large number of friends, each contributing some travel expenses (including meal expenses), and have one or two older people lead the way, and walk to a nearby town.

(2) Go to the countryside If you can't carry out the first item, then you can only invite three or five children to take a walk in the countryside. It is best to bring some bread and canned food, and eat around the ground in the suburbs, which is even more interesting.

(3) Parks If you are too far away from the countryside, you can go to several large parks. Good parks are no less tranquil and beautiful than the countryside. The benefits of a spring outing are about three kinds:

(1) Can increase knowledge

(2) Can increase literary inspiration

(3) Can regulate the spirit

(4) Children! Don't let the great spring escape!

The Adventures of Ah Huang (1) 213

— Ling Xuan

(1) "Ah! It's raining!" (2) "Take shelter under this tree!" (3) "Humph! Do you think I'm a tree?" (4) "Eh! It's you!"

Resisting Fate 214

— Jin Xi

According to a box of matches, "With a 'scratch' sound, the black spot is rubbed off on either side of the box, bursting out red light, dissipating our vitality, and gently falling to the ground. This is the final end of each of our compatriots. We are gladly willing to have such a fate."

What's strange is why a box of matches on the desk in the drawing-room would want to resist fate.

They also have a reason: "We are unwilling to be assigned by the master to burn cigarettes when smoking. This work cannot give the humans we love any benefit." As luck would have it, a mouse overturned a bottle of water at night, and the water splashed on them.

The next day, the master threw the box of matches out the door. Coincidentally, a child who collected old goods picked it up. The child put the box of matches on the stove to dry, restoring their lost abilities. From then on, the child cherished and assigned each match to do things when brewing tea and cooking rice.

Each match smiled contentedly: "Resisting fate, we have exhausted our greatest use."

Unable to Stand Firm 215

— Ruo Xu

Zhang'er and his father went out on a tram to buy things. When the tram started, almost everyone in the car fell backward. Later, when the tram stopped, the passengers almost fell forward again, as if they couldn't stand firm. Zhang'er was very strange and couldn't figure out the reason. Later, his father told him, "This is a problem of nature. Every object has a special property, and this property is called inertia, or laziness, which is 'if an object is moving, then it always likes to continue moving non-stop, and if it is not moving, then it is always still, unless there is another force to make trouble with it.' This property was discovered by Newton, a great scholar in England."

Zhang'er, hearing his father's words, unknowingly solved a doubt in his heart. Finally, his father told him again, "This phenomenon of inertia is originally very common, but because Newton can often pay attention to various common things in the world, he can become a famous scholar."

Teeth and Hygiene 216

— Han Yu

Children! Do you brush your teeth every day?

Children! You can now take a mirror and look at your teeth. Are your teeth white? Is there any tartar left? Are there any cavities? You have to pay attention to them.

Don't neglect your little teeth! They are very important for hygiene. If your teeth are not clean, they can destroy your teeth. Maybe they will then bring food into your body and destroy your stomach.

So, children, if you usually don't pay attention to your teeth, from now on, you have to start paying attention. Ask your dad or mom to buy a toothbrush and a bottle of toothpaste or tooth powder. The bristles on the toothbrush should be softer. You should brush once every night, morning, and after eating, so that food does not remain in your teeth and rot. After this becomes a habit, it will definitely be of great help to your health.

Small Jokes 217

— Li Yuan

Crow

During a drawing class, Mr. Chen discovered that one of the drawings submitted by the students was a piece of drawing paper completely covered in black ink. Mr. Chen didn't understand why.

Mr. Chen: "Who submitted this black paper?"

Wang'er: (Standing up) "It's me, sir."

Mr. Chen: "What did you draw?"

Wang'er: "It's a crow."

Mr. Chen: "This is all black ink, where is the crow?"

Wang'er: "Sir, this is a crow in the middle of the night!"

Mosquito Removal Method

The funny Ling'er often thinks he's smart. One summer evening, his father, mother, and brother were talking about the annoyance of mosquitoes and were eager for a method to remove them.

Ling'er's father: "Mosquitoes are really annoying. They suck our blood and buzz incessantly, making it impossible for us to sleep peacefully. Not only that, but sometimes they can also spread diseases! Ling'er," Dad asked with a smile, "Do you have any good ideas?"

Ling'er thought for a while and said, "Dad, I have an idea. Wine is such a fragrant thing! Now we immediately sprinkle some of it on the floor upstairs, so the mosquitoes will smell the fragrance and fly all the way upstairs, right? When they are all upstairs, we immediately take down the ladder, so they can't come down, right? Then we can sleep peacefully downstairs."

The Parrot's Death 218

— Wang Qianchuo

My family recently bought a parrot. It is very smart, so it has learned almost everything we usually say.

One day, when I was writing in the study, I suddenly heard the parrot shouting outside: "The cat is coming. The cat is coming. The cat is going to catch my tail feathers, what am I going to do!" I quickly ran outside to take a look. There was no cat there at all. It turned out that the parrot was joking.

Today I was in the study. I heard the parrot shouting outside again: "The cat is coming. The cat is coming. The cat is going to catch my tail feathers, what am I going to do!" I thought to myself: "Could it be that the parrot is joking with me again?" So I didn't go out to look. After a while, I walked outside. I saw that the parrot was really bitten to death on the ground by a cat!

Letter from a Rural Friend 219

— Zi Ming

Spring is here

Dear children:

The change of climate, the change of nature, in the city, one only feels the transition of "hot and cold," but in our countryside, it is unreserved. It changes at any time, and it shows us evidence at any time. The winter that has just passed not long ago, what it showed was a world of ice and snow, the trees took off their coats and hung silver fruit; the earth was desolate, bleak, and rigid. Now the season is "spring," but what evidence does it give us in the countryside?

Spring is here, here! We welcome it! But why is it so late? Spring! Don't you know? How many poor insects are left under the tyranny of "winter"! Children! The past winter is enough to be cursed and abandoned; this "spring" that drives away winter is worthy of our enthusiastic compliments and welcomes; however, what is spring?

The arrival of spring in our countryside does not require precise calculations by astronomical schools. Its arrival has its own hints for us. The morning frost, which is like white powder, has already rotted away, and instead there are bright, glistening beads. The wind, which blows coldly into the bones, has also subsided its power, and only gently and softly kisses people. Everything on the earth is preparing to move and be active in this world. There is a vigorous momentum here, and there will be many changes in the near future! Friends, I will report the news of spring later. I hereby make a reservation.

Women's Garden No. 5

The Back Wave 222

— Bi Yao

There are two ancient sayings that are as solid as gold and stone: "The back wave of the Yangtze River pushes the front wave, and new people in the world replace old people." This not only fully describes the rolling eastward flow of the Yangtze River and the ever-changing nature of human affairs and history, but even the single words "push" and "replace" are enough to show that the Yangtze River is "alive" and the world is also "alive."

Standing before the midnight of "March 18th," quietly reviewing the national liberation movement of the past few decades, especially the women's liberation movement, let's take a pen and draw an arc according to the degree of the movement. From the 20s of the Guangxu era, there was the enlightening natural foot movement, women's school movement, and the participation of Ms. Qiu Jin and others in the movement to overthrow the Manchu Qing dynasty. By the Xinhai year, there were women's northern expedition teams and women's military corps. After the establishment of the provisional government, although the women's army was disbanded, there was then the women's suffrage movement led by Tang Qunying and others. On March 19th of the first year of the Republic, because the Senate did not pass the women's suffrage bill, on the 20th there was a major disturbance in which women destroyed the Senate and kicked police officers. Since then, the women's movement of "imitating men" has gradually changed. Before long, the Chinese land came to a glacial era of Yuan Shikai. During this period, the world was not active, but just still. Not long after, waves arose on the calm water, colliding and stimulating each other, becoming a fierce new culture movement, with a sense of "Looking far ahead, a line of tide comes, pointing and looking back, snow forms into piles." At this time, the women's movement further put forward the slogans of "Destroying chastity! Destroying the old ethics!" Needless to say, in the national liberation movement during this period, such as in 1919 and 1926, women rationally demonstrated their strength. Women had already regarded themselves as social figures. During the Northern Expedition of 1926 and 1927, it can be said that without women, much of the effect would have been lost. The May 30th Massacre, the Shameen Massacre, and the "March 18th" resistance of all sectors of Beijing against the free navigation of the Eight-Nation Alliance on the Guhe River, each time many women were sacrificed. This period was the most intense period of the women's liberation movement, and also the most intense period of the national liberation movement. From this, we can see the complementary relationship between the two. From the 20s of the Guangxu era to the 16th and 17th years of the Republic of China, the women's movement rose higher and higher, and each generation was stronger than the previous one. At this time, the person holding the pen to draw the arc could simply throw down the pen and shout "Wonderful!"

However, the times for the women's movement are uneven, and now it happens to coincide with our incompetent generation, watching it decline and decline until it becomes still. Unable to continue the past, unable to usher in the future, what else can be said?

However, temporary phenomena will eventually overcome the permanent law of nature... equality and liberation are ultimately prescribed by the law of nature. In order to avenge the mournful cries of those abused maids, those devastated prostitutes, those tormented female workers, and other unfortunate women, we, the incompetent contemporary women, can only comfort them with shame and indignation, saying, "There is still a great back wave!"

New Life Movement and Modern Women 223

— Zi

China is a country where everything develops abnormally. Just taking daily life as an example, some people live in extreme luxury and enjoy themselves to the fullest. From birds and beasts to reptiles and snakes, they savor every delicacy and rare ingredient, earning themselves the reputation of being gourmets, known both domestically and abroad. They adorn themselves with fox fur, embroidered silk, and enjoy electric fans in their homes, unafraid of the harshness of nature, living as if in a perpetual spring breeze, in painted pavilions and carved buildings, high towers and grand mansions. They consume goods as if they were living in the 20th century, regardless of the fact that production levels are only at the 11th or 12th century level. On the other hand, most people lack adequate clothing and food. Some have no clothes to wear or food to eat. Thatched huts and the corners of pavilions and temples are their ideal residences. As for transportation, they are fortunate to have been given natural automobiles by their mothers, allowing them to travel freely, except on water or in the air. These are already common phenomena, so I don't need to elaborate further. As for solutions, there is the Principle of People's Livelihood.

What I want to talk about here is the New Life Movement, which I am reminded of by the above-mentioned lifestyles. Of course, every citizen of the Republic of China, regardless of gender or age, should abide by the New Life Movement. However, everything has its creators, practitioners, and those who follow their example. There is an ancient folk song that goes: "In the city, high buns are favored, so everywhere they are a foot high; in the city, large sleeves are favored, so everywhere a whole bolt of silk is used; in the city, wide eyebrows are favored, so everywhere they are shaved to half the forehead." This vividly depicts the phenomenon of those above influencing those below. Since the modern ladies and misses in the cities are able to follow the footsteps of Western women in every way, with their spirit of courageously improving and skillfully imitating, I believe that the modern class should be the vanguard in the beginning of this New Life Movement.

The goal of the New Life Movement is to make daily life and morality conform to propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame. Originally, "only when clothed and fed, do people know propriety and righteousness," but customs have changed since ancient times. Those who are clothed and fed have forgotten the ancient teachings of "propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame." To revive the nation, we should have something like the Blue Eagle movement in the United States, where everyone wears this badge and every item is marked with this symbol. However, ordinary village girls and rural women, though living in barren lands where clothing and food are scarce, may not necessarily violate ancient teachings. Their lives, though not up to par in terms of neatness and cleanliness, are already as simple and plain as possible. Before mankind invents eating air to satisfy hunger and wearing air to keep warm, there is no way to be any simpler or plainer. Therefore, I believe that the New Life Movement should especially be initiated by the modern ladies and misses who live leisurely lives. At that time, I can change the ancient folk song to: "In the city, frugality is favored, so everywhere people eat grass and fodder; in the city, plain clothes are favored, so everywhere people wear straw mats; in the city, makeup is discarded, so everywhere people remain yellow and black." In this way, with those above influencing those below, promoting the style of cleanliness and simplicity, and concurrently implementing other militarized and rationalized practices, it will truly be like what Chairman Chiang said, "At that time, whether it is to abolish all unequal treaties or to avenge our grievances and revive our nation, it will not be difficult."

Modern ladies and misses have the responsibility to lead women everywhere, because village girls and rural women, once they have your leisurely lives, will follow your lead, and perhaps even surpass you. At a time when there are few producers and many consumers, and you all abide by the ancient teachings, adhere to the maxim that men manage external affairs and women manage internal affairs, and comfortably reside among those who consume, judging from the general phenomenon, among the ranks of scholar-officials, comprador generals, and young masters, there is often one person supporting several families, new ones, old ones, official ones, unofficial ones, those without a name but with the reality of it. Among those being supported, except for a few of the old ones, everyone is qualified to be in the modern class, and the material enjoyment of the modern class is truly deserving of the name. On this day of shouting "propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame, revive the nation," I have high hopes for the modern class.

What Love Gave Me 224

— Linlin

Here is a bit of my life experience, which I write down to offer as a lesson to my young, unmarried female compatriots.

Six or seven years ago, I was a believer in the theory of "sacred love"; and believed that love was the most precious treasure in life, the only consolation; it could give people the greatest strength and courage to accomplish their great careers; it could also uplift depressed youth. So, before I could finish my studies, I married my current husband—my lover.

But, what was the situation after marriage? What did love give me? My husband did love me, and he planned my life very well, very stably. I got money from him, the so-called household expenses. Every day I was managing the cleanliness and beauty of our bedroom, the work of the kitchen, and the care of the children. Life after marriage was limited to these things. All the ideals before marriage, the desire for knowledge, were completely shattered. I was completely detached from society. The friends, relatives, neighbors, etc., I knew, they all used my husband's name to talk to me, they all interacted with me based on my husband's relationship. I understood very well that this was the title of appendage that I had created for myself, and put around my own neck. Because for that Ms. —, others did not treat her as an appendage of her husband, and interact with her. It was because she worked in a certain organization, because she had knowledge, because she had a specialty to directly participate in social undertakings! I have now become a cripple in knowledge and skills, and should be a domestic slave, an appendage of my husband, a parasite of society.

Now my husband is unemployed, and life is getting tighter day by day. Although we have saved money in every way, it is of no help. The family presents a gloomy picture, and the future is very bleak. My husband is frowning all day long. I try my best to comfort him, but that only adds more anxiety to him. Later, I also realized that this kind of comfort is not what he needs. He needs someone who can help him live and solve the pain of unemployment. But, but, I have become a cripple in knowledge, a cripple in skills, how can I solve it for him?

I now realize that love is not the only career in life, and love cannot be the guarantee of our lifelong life. It is only a small part of people's lives. Moreover, a woman should enrich her knowledge and complete her own specialized skills for earning a living before talking about love with a man, so that she can directly participate in all social production undertakings. Then you can avoid being an appendage of your future husband, a parasite of society, and you can also help your husband solve the difficulties, misfortunes, and unexpected encounters in the family. Your family will always be happy and blissful. You personally are independent and sound in society.

The New Female Type in Modern Literature 225

— Xu Xizhen

Modern intellectual women seem to have a beautiful longing... "to be a new person."

Saying "beautiful" actually has no satirical meaning at all. Under the current social system, the privilege of education seems to only remain among women of the petty bourgeoisie or above. Their only characteristic is that they like to build their world in the imagination of the future; and the ugly face of reality is inevitably hated.

So, in the beautiful world of imagination, they began to create a typical statue of the new woman.

The American writer Sinclair Lewis wrote a novel last year called "Ann Vickers." The bookstore advertisements prominently stated that this was Lewis's first novel with a female protagonist. Here, he wrote about American women in the ten years or so before and after the Great War. At that time, American intellectual women still had a very strong individualistic atmosphere. They loved freedom, loved activities, loved careers, and the so-called "social worker" was the most popular term at the time. Under the same social system, they built the same new female type... educated, dissatisfied with the current social system, full of transformative power, and full of emotion, they all wanted to be celebrities in society, hold the power of great careers in their hands, and be a modern savior in the ugly real world. They shouted to the public in a compassionate tone...

"Are you suffering? Don't shout, watch me fix it for you!"

But the public will not answer them for this kind of person, because they always only played the role of a god, a savior; they put their own position above the public.

Sinclair's observations may be correct. It is said that since this "Ann Vickers" was published, the sales have not been bad, and it has been loved by many intellectual women. What is especially moving is that at the end, the author still did not forget to put his Ann Vickers, who represented the American new woman of the early 20th century, into the circle of love.

In the works of the new American writer John Dos Passos, "Forty-Second Parallel" and "Nineteen Nineteen", we can also find the same type of new women.

And in fact, this represents all new women belonging to the intellectual class. This "new woman", in the pursuit of all careers, she always only played the role of a pitiful god - we can easily see the position of the god in the current society.

If we want to say it without mercy, modern women, no matter which group they belong to, have not achieved much success on the economic and social status battle lines. It is necessary to further study under the constraints of the family, the exercise of husband's power, and other bad social systems. From Gladkov's novel "Cement", we can see the outline of the new woman formed from the melting pot... the husband who left home for three years to participate in the war did not recognize the young wife at all when he returned. She could no longer endure the order to "come to bed!", and was no longer a virtuous housekeeper.

"There's hard bread and coffee, get it yourself, I still have a lot to do tomorrow," the wife said to her husband, who had been away for three years.

"What the hell have you seen?"

This is really a magical magic, three years of time, turning a young woman into this appearance.

But precisely because this is the training obtained from human society, and this training may be necessary for modern new women.

Of course, I don't want to define a model for the new woman, that is fundamentally boring; but modern new women should be liberated from housework, and strive to obtain equal status with men in economic, cultural, and other conditions, and equally do something more meaningful, it seems necessary, right?

World Famous Women

Mrs. Ninnepeng, Danish Minister of Education 226

— Xuewen

The general public's view of the two sexes cannot get rid of the following prejudice: that women and men have various differences in ability. When women handle something, they rarely have their own opinions, and blindly follow others, "repeating what others say," and are "irresolute" in doing things, etc. However, looking at Mrs. Ninnepeng's handling methods, we can now know that this is not right.

She is Danish and has served as the Minister of Education in Denmark. When she took office, a reporter from an American magazine criticized her like this... "She is female and radical!" We can know what kind of person she is from this criticism.

Two things people dare not do...

Shortly after taking office, she did two things that people did not dare to do.

The first thing was to dismiss the directors of the Royal Theater. In Denmark, there was originally a great national art institution called the Royal Theater. Inside, there were many famous works from ancient and modern times, as well as a large group of theater troupes and dance teams. It had a very long history and reputation in the country. However, according to the inherited regulations, the four directors of this theater had to call someone with the title of count to be the director. However, each count could not concentrate on the duties of the theater, and the other directors took this opportunity to muddle through. As a result, the inside of the theater became extremely corrupt, even having its form but only embracing the false name of history. When Mrs. Ninnepeng took office, she greatly disagreed with this situation. As a result, she dismissed the count and the directors who were not working effectively, and only retained one director who was competent, and ordered him to concentrate on running it, so the theater was rectified.

As for that poor count, she simply said he was "useless dust."

The second thing was to ban the interference of the parish in schools. In Denmark, the power of the church originally spread everywhere, and the pastors of each parish had the special right to inspect schools. If the school did not teach religious subjects effectively, it would be punished by the parish. As a result, every lively child's mind was made dull by religious subjects. After Mrs. Ninnepeng took office, she again greatly disagreed with this, and on the one hand, she vigorously supported the teachers' union to oppose the church's inspection; on the other hand, she ordered the director of the teachers' training institute to be dismissed. In this way, the inherited power of the parish over the school was invisibly eliminated.

These two things were things that previous Danish Ministers of Education dared not do, but she actually implemented them according to her own views.

Her biography...

Mrs. Ninnepeng has done many other things. She was born in 1866 and joined the Social Democratic Party early on. She obtained a master's degree from a famous university in Copenhagen. In 1903, she served as the clerk of the Social Democratic Party headquarters. In 1917, she worked for the Copenhagen Bureau of Industry. In 1918, she became a member of the Upper House. She has many writings, about history and economics. Her husband is a doctor of philosophy and is also enthusiastic about the social democratic movement.

Overview of Women's Lives in Gaiping County, Liaoning 227

— Zhibai

—A glimpse of women's lives in the interior of our country—

Gaiping County, Liaoning, is a place where Han, Manchu, and Hui people live together. The Han people account for about two-thirds, the Manchu people are fewer, and the Hui people are the least. Therefore, customs and habits are gradually assimilated by the Han people. Moreover, they intermarry, and the inherent customs become mixed. The situation of women of all ethnic groups rarely shows inherent and different traces. Now, I will briefly write a systematic narrative of the women's lives in this area, to offer to those who love to know the customs and human feelings of various places.

(1) Family

Women in Gaiping County, Liaoning, have the following responsibilities in the family: to be filial and obedient to elders, to be tolerant and respectful to peers, and to nurture and teach younger generations. Their minds are full of good ideas such as "virtuous daughter-in-law," "virtuous lady," and "virtuous wife and loving mother." They are bound by the old chains—the three obediences and four virtues, and the husband sings, the wife follows. They must listen to the commands and teachings of their husbands in everything. In the family, they are in a position to be directed, and they do not get some rights. But they do not argue. The idea of "equal rights for men and women" has never entered their minds.

(2) Knowledge

Because education is not popular, there are only a few simple female teachers, higher primary schools, and lower primary schools in Gaiping County. Male schools do not recruit female students, and female schools do not recruit male students. There are no female schools in the countryside. People all uphold the old morality that "a woman's lack of talent is a virtue," and the poor are even more unable to afford to go to school, so women who have received education are like phoenix feathers and unicorn horns. The general women are uneducated, vulgar, and do not understand worldly affairs. Their minds are filled with stories from Biographies of Heroic Women, Collections of Famous Sages, and Women's Moral Classics. New knowledge will not invade their minds.

(3) Clothing and Decoration

Most Han women wear short clothes, and a small number still bind their feet—although foot binding has been banned, many people still bind their feet—most Manchu and Hui women wear cheongsams and have natural feet. Han women comb their hair in a bun style, while Manchu and Hui women comb their hair in a large bouffant style. These still preserve obvious traces of ethnicity. As for women who cut their hair, they are rarely seen in Gaiping County. They wear flowers on their heads, apply powder to their faces, lipstick to their lips, and wear embroidered shoes on their feet. With such decorations, their hearts are filled with infinite beauty, they linger in front of the mirror, as if they were celestial beings, and their faces show an arrogant look. They also show off to others and can also please others.

(4) Frugality and Hard Work

The women of Gaiping County are very simple and frugal with money. They wear cloth clothes and cloth shoes and walk on foot. They have the virtue of frugality. In the spring, they sow seeds on the ground like men. In the summer, under the hot sun, they hoe the ground like men. In the autumn, they go to the fields and the threshing floor, working desperately. In the winter, because there is nothing to do in the fields, they are still constantly engaged in needlework, spinning hemp ropes, etc., at home. Their hard work is no less than that of men, and this spirit is truly admirable.

(5) Occupation

Gaiping County is mainly agricultural, and most women work at home. Because it is easy to live and they are bound by old morals, women cannot go out to work. Only when they are extremely poor and have no choice do they become female workers. Women can make hemp ropes, spin thread, spin cattle hair, and do needlework in their spare time at home, which can earn them a few silver coins, which is commonly called making up for "the expenses of shoes, heads, and feet." This can be considered their extra occupation—or their side business.

(6) Customs Sketch

As a rule, throughout the entire first month of the year, women stop working and avoid moving needles and threads. They come up with all sorts of strange ways to pass the time. Like inviting the Kitchen God Aunt, using the method of kowtowing to predict the good or bad of the year. On the seventh day of the first month, women have to eat radishes—said to be able to prevent toothache for a year. On the night of the fifteenth day of the first month, they all go ice skating, which can prevent leg pain for a year. There are too many of these ridiculous superstitious things. They most believe in fortune-telling blind men. In a month, they often want to have their fortunes told. They are not stingy with this kind of expense. Women cannot visit their parents' home after the twenty-second day of the twelfth month—for fear of harming their parents' family. Before the sixth day of the first month, women cannot look at the offerings and cured meat on the ancestors' altar in their parents' home—looking at it is detrimental to their parents' family—if women sew clothes on their bodies (without taking off their clothes), they must hold a pipe in their mouths—for fear of others accusing them of being thieves. This is just a glimpse of the customs of women in Gaiping County. The above six sections are the outline of women's lives in Gaiping County.

A Woman's Life 229

— Xuanwen

4. Selection of a Spouse

—Whether the other party has a venereal disease—

Of course, there are many conditions for choosing a spouse, such as the other party's personality, knowledge, economic ability, and health status. These should all be carefully considered. Now, I will only discuss the health aspect... From the perspective of heredity and eugenics, people with tuberculosis, leprosy, and venereal diseases should absolutely avoid marrying. Among them, venereal disease is the most terrible... Therefore, when choosing a spouse, the first condition should be to be absolutely free from venereal disease. There are many women in the world who silently lead unhappy and painful lives because their husbands have venereal diseases.

Because of the difference in physiological organization between men and women, men tend to be dynamic and cannot easily live a life of abstinence. However, under the current social system, because it is not easy to make a living, men are often unable to marry or marry late. As a result, the risk rate of venereal diseases also increases. Examining the treatment of venereal diseases, it is very difficult. It takes a considerable amount of time and money to be completely cured, and once the treatment is interrupted, there is a risk that it cannot be eradicated. If a woman marries such a man, what will her pain be like? Therefore, before marriage, a reliable doctor should be asked to issue a health certificate, which should be exchanged with each other. This is a necessary procedure to be followed before marriage. If a couple in love is approaching the wedding date, and the man knows that he has a venereal disease, he should inform the woman before marriage, and then remarry only after the doctor proves that he has been completely cured.

Last year, a so-called marriage cancellation issue occurred in Japan. The fact is that there was a couple in love who, with the agreement of both parents, chose a date to marry. After a solemn and lively wedding ceremony, the woman discovered on the wedding night that the man had a venereal disease. She immediately announced it to both families and proposed to cancel the marriage contract. At that time, the guests had not yet dispersed and were shocked to hear the news. However, the woman abruptly and resolutely said that it must be canceled immediately. In the end, the marriage contract was canceled in public, and she returned to her mother's home with her pure heart and body. This news spread throughout Japan last year, and the general public opinion believed that it was a rational new woman's unyielding and proper means, and a blow to irresponsible men.

Commercial News

Financial News: Gold Price Drops 5.5 Yuan 230

American Bank Representative to Present Opinion on Monday

After the previous day's sharp rise in the gold market, the American Bank failed to offer lower prices yesterday, and instead prices rebounded. While this was expected, the upward trend was inevitably halted. The exchange market eased, and retail investors took the opportunity to sell small amounts, leading to a decline. The fluctuation range during the morning session was narrow. At the opening, due to the unified decline in the British and American silver markets, the closing price of forward silver on the Five Metals Exchange rose by 3 to 5 percent. Exchange rates slightly contracted. London spot gold rose by one penny, American cotton fell by sixteen pounds, while American wheat rose by three and seventy-five hundredths. (Hu Bei) Yesterday, thirty-two or three boats arrived from various merchants downstream. The sales appetite of various goods in the market turned dull, and the market price of white japonica rice was stable. Early rice and thin rice prices were cut by several fen. Yangjian was also flat and weak. Du Bu, Ke Jian, and Bian Yin Yuan saw no significant changes.

Peanut Market Turns Active 247

The peanut market had been sluggish for a long time. Yesterday, the market atmosphere began to turn active. This was because foreign firms in Qingdao moved to increase prices, so the Guangdong market also improved. Local purchasing demand increased sharply, and the city's total transaction volume was about 400 tons. The selling price of Xuzhou goods was 3 yuan, 7 jiao, and 5 fen to 7 jiao. Guide goods opened at 3 yuan, 8 jiao, and 5 fen to 8 jiao. Lanfeng goods were quoted at 4 yuan, and Kaifeng goods were at 4 yuan and 1 jiao. Peanut sales have declined recently, so market prices continue to weaken, it is said.

Metals 248

New Stock of English Tinplate Arrives

The long-awaited 90-pound English tinplate, its new stock of over 2,000 boxes, arrived at the Xin Tai Gu Wharf yesterday. Therefore, customers who generally purchase this product rushed to buy it upon hearing the news. It is said that over 500 boxes have been sold, with a price of 15 yuan and 1 jiao per box, which is slightly less than the American product by two to three jiao. However, the exchange rate has been shrinking recently, so market conditions have not declined.

Shen Bao Amateur Weekly

The Suicide Problem 268

— Yi Ping

All of people's efforts and struggles are for the sake of one word: "life." In our era, even those who are penniless must beg and plead for scraps to survive. As for the wealthy, they naturally want to live forever and enjoy an extremely comfortable life. Life, whether rich or poor, is something everyone truly craves.

Yet, strangely, there are many living people in the world who commit suicide! In recent years, the number of suicides in China has been increasing day by day. In Shanghai alone, on average, several suicide news items are published in various newspapers every week. What is the reason for this? Generally, this problem is superficially understood from the perspective of the individual suicide victim. If the suicide victim committed suicide due to a broken heart, it is said that the reason lies in the heartbreak. If the suicide victim committed suicide due to economic oppression, it is said that the reason lies in economic oppression. But the problem is not as simple as that.

First, we should know that among countless suicide victims, regardless of how different the direct causes of their suicides may be, regardless of how different their suicide methods may be, there is one thing they have in common: that is, their suicide is due to their feeling hopeless about everything. If a person still has a glimmer of hope, if there is still a ray of light in front of them, I dare say that they would never commit suicide no matter what.

Hope, although it can be said to be a kind of human instinct, is determined by the social environment in which they live. The hopes of doctors and prostitutes are different, the hopes of movie stars and tofu-selling girls are different, and the hopes of warlords, corrupt officials, and the common people clash. The reason for this is that their living environments are different. Therefore, a person's despairing suicide is actually produced by the society in which they live. Suicide due to being unable to resist economic oppression is naturally due to the fact that the society in which they live cannot provide them with relative economic satisfaction. Suicide due to feeling hopeless about the future of the country is even more inextricably linked to the society in which they live. Even young men and women who commit suicide due to heartbreak do so because they feel that everything else in the society in which they live is of no great significance, forming a concept of love as the primary meaning of life. Therefore, once they lose their love, they feel that everything is over, that the universe and life have no meaning at all, and that the only option is suicide....

Therefore, we can say that if a country or a society has a larger number of suicides, it is all the more proof that the morbidity of this society is serious, and that it cannot satisfy the majority of people, causing many people to feel disappointed and commit suicide. In China today, not only is the number of suicides increasing day by day, but the scope of suicides is also expanding. It has now expanded from coolies, merchants, and prostitutes to poets and movie stars. The former is exemplified by the poet Zhu Xiang's drowning, and now there is the movie star Ai Xia's poisoning. These shocking facts fully illustrate how the current Chinese society is destroying the lives of many people, and how deep the root cause of the problem has become.

However, although the cause of suicide lies in the morbidity of society, the act of suicide is not a heroic expression. Suicides are, in reality, cowards. If the morbid society of China today produces many suicide tragedies, then the suicides of many people under this are cowardly expressions of their inability to resist the attacks of this society!

Life

Our Writer 269

— Lun Liu

Our writer opened a major magazine's submission guidelines and looked at them excitedly.

"Three yuan a day! Thirty yuan for ten thousand words!"

So, he started taking out his pen. Writing requires ink, so our author searched for a bottle of Min Sheng brand blue ink stained with dirt at the bottom of the table. But the bottle was already empty. Our author cursed "Damn it!" and took out two dimes from his tattered suit pocket, and then ran out of his small room. Next, he ran back and picked up the thermos. He said softly, "I have to write good articles... be happy and healthy, make money... this is capital."

Our author came back from the public stove after getting hot water. Now, he was thinking about what kind of article to write. Unconsciously, he returned to his small room. He had ink, he had tea, but a bald head stretched in from the corner of the door. Our writer frowned, but then he realized that this head had power, it was the landlord's face demanding money, and he had no choice but to stand up. The bald head spoke first...

"Hey! - Two months of rent hasn't been paid. We can't live on air. Otherwise, everyone will lose face. You are a scholar..."

He couldn't speak. In fact, he was still planning to write 15,000 words! Send it today, receive it the day after tomorrow, maybe the editor will like me, and tomorrow, the day after tomorrow, there will be a response, so he spoke with some backbone...

"Today is the 7th, I will definitely pay it off by the 10th, sixteen yuan, not a single penny less!"

With that, the landlord started to roll out, and he closed the door.

"Okay, I'll see you on the 10th..." The words below were not clear. Forget about it, our writer quickly wrote the article, lest he get angry!

Next door, a radio suddenly turned on, a three-tube machine - the sound was noisy enough. And there were several tactless women laughing wildly.

"...rocking...baby...want to...sleep."

Our writer dropped his pen, took out a cigarette, and threw away the empty pack. He also stopped thinking about what kind of novel to write and started cursing...

"This kind of star, hey, shameless. Still - broadcasting what sound! ..."

He wanted to keep cursing, but the radio next door turned up again, the sound was even more unpleasant.

"...My baby, my baby..."

Those women also made their voices shrill at the same time, it was a sound that made people's hair stand on end, and after a while, they laughed wildly again.

Our writer sighed, and sullenly slipped out of his small room. He slapped the table and said heavily...

"——Going to find material!" Temporarily, he also took a major magazine.

Late at night, after spending fifteen copper coins to eat a bowl of plain noodles, our writer returned to his small room. Now, he was already carrying a heavy fatigue, not caring about anything, putting it off until tomorrow, wanting to sleep was the nature of a writer. Our writer fell asleep snoring.

Tomorrow, the calendar reads "8". Our writer washed his face with water he got from the public stove, sipped his tea, and picked up his pen. But yesterday, he "dawdled" for a long time, and couldn't find any good material for a novel to submit. If our writer could throw sixteen yuan on the table, the landlord would take it away with great importance without saying a word, how majestic that would be - in this way, our writer made a gesture with his pen on the paper he had just laid out.

"Now, articles must grasp modernity. Or write a novel about war!" But our writer had never seen a war. When Shanghai was fighting, our writer also escaped home to spend a year. So he wanted to use another kind of material to write an article.

Page 20

"Popular articles - the latest style, proletarian literature..." He also thought of describing the background of rural collapse.

Our writer wrote the two words "Autumn Harvest" on the first line of the manuscript paper, but he also thought that this theme was too common, so he immediately tore it to shreds. At this time, he remembered the rent again, and he only had one silver dollar on him.

As a result, our writer wrote an article called "Year-End". He described the suffering of a farmer, and the year-end hardships in the bankrupt countryside. Although he didn't understand how difficult the year-end was for farmers, he yawned triumphantly, and broke two pen tips. This was a capital of 14,000 words and forty yuan. It was already the 9th, and tomorrow, he had to pay off the hard words from the day before. So our writer cleverly wrote a letter to the editor, saying that he had to leave for Hangzhou the day after tomorrow, and asked for the payment to be sent immediately. He also personally went to the post office to affix the postage, double registered!

On the 10th, our writer opened his eyes and it was already eleven o'clock. A person was pushed into the small room, and he thought...

"Has the payment arrived?"

But——a bald head, with two energetic eyes looking at him.

"Ha! Let me go to my friend Mr. Li's place to get the money today..."

The bald head couldn't speak, he only slowly swallowed a sentence and left, this sentence was an ambiguous word containing half irony and half hope, the sound seemed to have not dissipated...

"See...if...you...don't...break your promise!"

Our writer jumped out of bed, rummaged through the boxes but found nothing to pawn, so he went out. He did not leave the vicinity of his small room, he was afraid that the person sending the payment would deliver it to the wrong address. It was not until the afternoon that he saw the postman knocking on the door, and our writer's heart was boiling. He quickly ran to the door where the postman was standing, and saw a large roll, he couldn't speak, he just shouted... "Give it to me, give it to me."

When our writer received his masterpiece returned intact, he was disheartened. He did not unpack the rejected manuscript. He just shouted... "....Introducing new works, deceiving people, damn it, just teasing me."

He had no relatives here, only a few poor friends, who also traded in submissions. Our writer was now running on a purposeless road, the bald head's ambiguous words had not yet dissipated...

"See...if...you...don't...break your promise!"

This, our writer couldn't care about, later, he didn't return to his small room.

International Broadcasting Radio Station

British Military Expansion Fever 270

— Qing Lin

According to the British aircraft industry's mouthpiece "Aircraft," all British aircraft manufacturers made substantial profits last year (1933). Fairey Aviation Co, famous for manufacturing military aircraft, increased its profits by 12.5 percent in 1933. Rolls-Royce Co, which specializes in manufacturing motors for British military aircraft, increased its profits by 5.5 percent. British aircraft production also increased last year. Hawker Engineering Co has recently set up a new company to operate this thriving business. And according to the company's boss, Mr. S. P. Cigg, the number of aircraft produced last year broke the record of the past few years after the war. The reason why the British aircraft industry can be particularly prosperous in this year of economic depression is naturally due to Britain's fervent military expansion. Last year, Britain's air force expenditure was 17,426,000 pounds, expenditure on the army was 37,950,000 pounds (an increase of 1,462,000 pounds compared to 1932), and navy expenditure was 53,370,000 pounds (an increase of 3 million pounds compared to 1932).

Britain has also repeatedly conducted experiments on controlling aircraft by radio. It is said that several inventions in this area have been secretly patented. The year before last, Vickers Arinsttong obtained patents for new aircraft guns, bomb-dropping and bomb-throwing machines, etc. And last year, several inventions concerning anti-aircraft guns and machine guns were also patented.

Recently, the British cavalry regiment was reorganized into a tank regiment, and the combat power of the original tank battalions has been strengthened. The armored vehicle regiment has also been reorganized. In short, the British army's three-year mechanization plan is progressing step by step, with new completions every year.

Britain is also making every effort in the preparation for chemical warfare. Under the leadership of military authorities and specially appointed chemical experts, military chemical research is underway. Among its recent achievements, the important ones are complete gas masks and a new type of poison gas. Naturally, the British government's expenditure of 105,000 pounds on this "scientific endeavor" last year will not be without a price.

In addition, various experiments on naval, land and air force equipment are also frequently held. Last year, Britain spent 758,000 pounds on naval experiments, 615,000 pounds on army experiments, and 1,385,000 pounds on air force experiments.

However, the British media still do not consider this kind of fervent arms expansion to be sufficient, and they often hysterically say that Britain's military equipment is insufficient. The Daily Mail even listed figures, pointing out that Britain ranks only fifth among the major powers in terms of air force, and advocating the immediate construction of 3,000 aircraft. Last year, the Conservative Party (the current ruling party in Britain) annual meeting also passed a resolution approving this proposal.

It seems that British aircraft factories will undoubtedly have a good year this year. (According to the British Esperanto News Agency)

Wandering Daughter 271

— Ms. Zhu

This is neither a whirlpool of the turbulent times, nor a storm in history; this is a small bubble that disappears in the vast sea of people. It is not worth remembering, nor worth sighing; but it is hateful that it often comes to mind in my heart! In the year of the eighteenth century's death under the grinding wheels of history, it was a great famine year. At that time, the best white rice sold for no more than five thousand coins per dan, and dried tofu was still two small coins a piece, but the news of people starving to death was no longer anything to talk about. It was at that time that my mother fell into my father's home. Although my father was such a kind and benevolent person, and that mother who died ten years earlier! The so-called legitimate mother, was also equally gentle and amiable; but, undoubtedly, my mother lived a life of cattle, horses and slaves. Living in the old family of feudal society, my mother continued to bear the burden of household labor and life for the next thirty years. However, in people's eyes, there was no place for the mother in the so-called "human" realm. Although she could work and give birth, she was regarded as a living meat machine in the family; she could not be regarded as a member of society. Such a view has not only become the "golden rule" in the past society, but also has its explicit basis in the law today! Where can my mother obtain the qualification of a "person"? I can't help but cry out for my mother, and shout out for the thousands of oppressed women in the old society!

Unexpectedly, I only shouted this once, and I had to leave my mother again for six years.

It has been almost two years since I had any news of my mother. Needless to say, I could not enjoy the greatest maternal love in the world, and I could not even receive news of my mother's daily life, which could usually give me some comfort; what loss and heartache in life is greater than this? My spiritual God! Bless my mother! People all over the world who are far away from their loving mothers, let us bless the mothers of the world!

I remember in the harsh winter of 1931, a letter from my mother was sent from my hometown, with the following passage...

"...Since you left, slander has gathered on me. The clansmen disapprove of what you have done, and hate me as a result, and add insult to injury, deceiving, enticing, and threatening in many ways, trying to seize your father's inheritance. I am old and weak, and you have no brothers, and I am lonely and helpless, so it is difficult to contend with them. At this time, the weather is cold and the year is coming to an end, and I have no means of livelihood, and I am destined to starve to death. I have no choice but to give up everything and leave my hometown to go to your uncle's house, to end this remaining life. Your future is bright, I hope you will not think of me as a candle in the wind, and harm your body; fortunately..."

At that time, when I read this letter, tears streamed down my face, and my heart was shattered, and I almost fainted; the heartache and resentment at that time were truly indescribable. I think my tears were almost exhausted for this time, so in the past two years, although I have also thought of her and my heart aches, and I have even encountered repeated difficulties and even sometimes thought of committing suicide, I have never shed a tear again.

I do not have a fixed address, and my uncle's house is a rural village without postal service; although there are so-called relatives and friends in my hometown, they all treat me as a rebellious enemy; in this way, my mother's news is like a lone boat sunk in the sea, making it impossible for me to explore.

Originally, all of my mother's hardships were bestowed by the current social system, and I should naturally not be held responsible; however, now that she is "destined to starve to death", can I say that I should not be held responsible? How heartbreaking this is! But, what can I do? I think, under this social system, if the children of countless mothers are unwilling to sell their souls and cannot exploit the blood and sweat of others, can they really "lie on ice to seek carp" or "cry bamboo to grow bamboo shoots" to show filial piety to their mothers? Even if these things are possible; their mothers would never let their children do them, right?

How empty and how painful is the heart of a poor person's mother!

When I think of my mother, I curse the old society; it not only makes millions of people starve and suffer, but also destroys the most precious love between fathers and sons and between mothers and daughters without leaving a trace.

"Although my hometown is good, I don't think of returning" This truly reveals my heart. In fact, not to mention that there is nothing worth cherishing in my hometown, where else in this world, except for that pure land that I yearn for, is there a place for me to stand? Here, I can't help but recall Yang Sao's poems...

"My heart is leisurely, I don't know where to go, I don't know where to stay?

While I am still young, I will do my best to wander; if I grow old, I will die!! Die in the heart of heaven and earth!"

Amateur Entertainment

Splashing Water on a Bottle 272

— White Goose

This is a physics-based game, but the method is very simple and the principle is also easy to understand.

Method: Take a white glass bottle, fill it with a little more than half water, and place it in a pot of salt water to boil. After the water in the pot boils, and the water in the bottle boils as well, put on the stopper, remove the bottle, and place it horizontally on the table (at this time, the water is no longer boiling). Then, take a glass of cold water and splash it on the bottle, and the water inside the bottle will boil again. Splash another glass, and it will boil again in the same way.

Reason: Ordinarily, if the water in a bottle is placed in fresh water and boiled, the water in the bottle will not boil; after adding salt, the temperature of the salt water will be higher than one hundred degrees depending on the amount of salt, so the water in the bottle also boils. After boiling, the air inside the bottle is completely expelled by the water vapor. To prevent air from entering again, the stopper is put on. After splashing cold water, the water vapor inside the bottle condenses into water droplets, so the atmospheric pressure above the water in the bottle is reduced. Because the lower the pressure on the water surface, the lower the boiling point of the water, so even without adding more fire, the water boils again.

European Problems and Pacific Problems 273

— Yang Wenzhi

After the First World War of 1914 and 1928, the imperialist powers re-divided the world. In Europe, it was the Treaty of the Versailles Peace Conference; in the Americas, it was the agreement of the Washington Conference. However, the situations created by these two international conferences are now outdated and no longer correspond to the balance of power between the imperialist powers. Because the law of uneven development of capitalism has shown its effect particularly powerfully after the European war. The situation of uneven development is very obviously manifested in the era of the general crisis of capitalism. And in the third period of the general crisis today—the deepening of the global economic panic—the force of uneven development has been further strengthened. The period of relative stability of capitalism has ended. Huge conflicting forces are developing as much as possible, and the current world is approaching the door of war. Re-dividing the world through war is the current problem for the imperialist powers. Now, let's try to briefly discuss the main focal points of conflict between imperialists.

European Problems: The temporary victory of Fascist Germany has further promoted the crisis of armed conflict. The fuse of war has already been lit. Fascist Germany demands revision of the Treaty of Versailles. It demands the return of Danzig (the Polish Corridor) and the Saar. This corridor issue could trigger an outbreak of war at any time, because France (the de facto master of Poland) will not easily allow Germany to gain a new and economically important seaport in Western Europe.

At the same time, the Austrian problem is also one of the most important issues in revising the Treaty of Versailles. Fascist Germany openly demands the "annexation of Austria." Because if Austria and Germany merge, German imperialism can reach out to seize the sphere of influence in the Balkan Peninsula and the Near East, such as Turkey, and surround Czechoslovakia on three sides, and raise the issue of incorporating the three million Germans in Czechoslovakia into Germany, and can also place Hungary under its own influence. The merger of Austria and Germany can take two forms: one is open annexation; the other is "unification" annexation, i.e., the Nazi Party of Hitler's faction seizes power in Austria. However, these plans are not only seen by the French bourgeoisie as the "fuse of a new war" from the merger of Austria and Germany, but also opposed by Fascist Italy. Although Italy is united with Germany on other issues, it opposes and undermines Germany's plans in this matter. The recent meeting of Italy, Austria, and Hungary is one of the tricks played by Italy. But the Austrian problem is actually only a part of the Danube problem. Italy wants to merge Austria and Hungary, and if possible, also wants to merge Croatia of Yugoslavia, and place these places under its leadership. France wants to incorporate Austria and Hungary into the Little Entente, creating a "Danube Federation." And Hungary demands revision of the Treaty of Trianon, ceding some territories of Yugoslavia, Romania, and Czechoslovakia. Italy supports Hungary's plan, but these three Little Entente countries, relying on the power of France, are unwilling to give in.

The Danube problem and the Balkan problem are closely linked. Italy wants to divide Yugoslavia, ceding Croatia, seizing Dalmatia (the islands on the Adriatic coast), and turning the Adriatic Sea into Italy's "inland sea." At the same time, Italy also wants to resolve the long-standing disputes on the Balkan Peninsula, the conflict between Yugoslavia, Bulgaria, and Greece—the Albanian problem. Italy advocates handing over Albania to Bulgaria and Greece.

The dispute between Germany and Poland over Danzig and Upper Silesia is actually a conflict between Germany and France. Similarly, the dispute between Italy and Yugoslavia is actually a conflict between Italy and France. The latter also has the North African problem. France and Italy are both vying for leadership in the Mediterranean, vying for the sphere of influence in Savoy and Nice, as well as in the Near East.

The imperialist powers are all frantically arming themselves, preparing for a new imperialist war to resolve their conflicts. But at the same time, the imperialists are also attempting to use the armament they are preparing to attack the Soviet Union in order to alleviate the contradictions between the imperialists. Regarding the issue of the merger of Austria and Germany, due to the opposition of France and Italy, the semi-official newspaper of the German Fascist Foreign Ministry openly published the idea of "unifying Ukraine," because part of the territory of Ukraine belongs to the Soviet Ukrainian Republic. And British imperialism secretly supports Japan's annexation of Manchuria and Mongolia in its Far East policy; and in its European policy, it supports Germany's radical anti-Soviet Union stance. In fact, British imperialism has now replaced the position of French imperialism and become the main organizer of the anti-Soviet Union war. Pacific Problems: In the Pacific, the imperialist division of China is already underway.

Japanese imperialism has already occupied the three northeastern provinces, Jehol, and part of Chahar, and is continuing to invade the Pingjin area and preparing to invade Outer Mongolia. Japan has built new naval bases on the Caroline and Ogasawara Islands, which were administered by Germany. Japan is also trying to create a "Dungan state" of nationalities around Dihua.

British imperialism is also invading China. South China is the sphere of influence of British imperialism. It is also seizing Tibet and Xikang to seize Sichuan. The recent independence of southern Xinjiang was manipulated by British imperialism.

French imperialism is active in southern Sichuan through Annam, traversing Yunnan, and Guizhou. The recent news that British troops entered Yunnan is a demonstration by British imperialism to French imperialism.

American imperialism has already lent China 50 million US dollars in cotton and wheat loans, etc.

Due to the conflicts caused by the imperialist division of China, the naval race in the Pacific is becoming extremely tense. But the main reason for the tense naval race is to attack China and deal with the Soviet Union. The United States has passed a bill to expand the navy—naval expenditures have increased to 1,000,000,000 US dollars—and has decided to build two naval bases each in the Atlantic and Pacific Oceans, and also to "survey" the Aleutian Islands. Britain has also passed a naval budget of £56,550,000—an increase of £2,980,000 over last year—and is rushing to build the Singapore naval base and buying Timor Island. France has also occupied nine small islands in the South China Sea of ​​China and is stepping up the construction of military projects. Japan has also passed the budget for the second supplementary naval plan.

Japan's military actions in China and the war between the small countries in South America are preludes to the imminent new world war!

Book and Newspaper Chronicle

After Reading "Elementary School Natural Science Vocabulary Book" 274

— Yunshan

The Shen Bao's advertisement on the 5th stated that the Commercial Press published the "Elementary School Natural Science Vocabulary Book." I was overjoyed because this type of comprehensive dictionary can be said to be an unprecedented book. I immediately went to Qipan Street to buy one. After flipping through it hastily, I was very disappointed. I will write some of it to tell everyone.

(1) Content: Miscellaneous. This book is named Natural Science Vocabulary Book, so it should be a specialized vocabulary book. It should not collect many non-natural science nouns to fill the number. We can see that it is miscellaneous and impure from the twenty-three categories in its classification index. What is even more ridiculous is that the "Games" category is also included.

(2) Inverted Sequence. On the fourth page of the table of contents, the character "芫" is suddenly listed. According to the "芫" character system, it should not be included in the nine strokes, especially the number on page "six zero three" should not be inserted under "three nine six" for no reason. After checking the main text, the character "芫" is actually arranged in the eleven strokes. Is this not an inverted sequence?

(3) Inaccurate Classification. In the "Chemical Industry" category on page 20 of the classification index, there is "Opium," and there is also "Opium" on page 21. After checking the main text, there is "Opium" on page "seven four two," and there is "Opium" on page "nine seven five." This is a repetition, so it does not hurt much. However, there is also an entry of "Cloud" in the same category on the same page, which cannot be understood no matter how much I think about it. Does this vocabulary book have the ability to create "Clouds" by using "Chemical Industry"?

(4) Inappropriate Material Selection. The material selection of this book is inappropriate. Some extremely important nouns are missing, while "Inkstone" and "Brush" (see pages 703 and 705), which are not very relevant to natural science, are included in the book, which is quite inappropriate. Moreover, the annotations under these two nouns purely focus on historical narratives and have no scientific explanation.

(5) Inaccurate Proofreading. Accuracy is the most important thing for a vocabulary book. If there are many errors, it is not only useless but also harmful. The proofreading of this book is inaccurate, and typos are often seen, which is a major shortcoming.

In short, this book is a crudely made product. Although the quantity is large, the quality is very poor. There are only more than 200 entries of "Chemical Part" nouns. The rest can be seen. The reporter hopes that the museum can maintain its historical glory, take this book as a warning, and pay more attention to the substantial aspects of future books. It is not only beneficial to the public, but also beneficial to the museum itself. I don't know what the museum authorities think?

Commentary

Defects of the Rent Reduction Movement Itself 275

— Wu Mao

I am someone who lives in an attic room, so according to the usual practice of "three sentences without leaving the topic," my words are completely based on the interests of those who live in attic rooms.

Recently, the rent reduction movement in this city has spread like a storm. Many enlightened people have already discussed the inevitability and importance of this movement, so there is no need for me to add anything more. However, I always feel that there are some defects in the movement itself, that is, I have not seen anyone living in an attic room in any alley participating in an organized way.

Is it that people living in attic rooms do not need rent reduction? No! The so-called people living in attic rooms probably include shop assistants, workers, and other wage laborers, as well as various groups of unemployed and out-of-school people. Their incomes are very meager, or even have no income at all. Although the world economic panic and imperialist dumping have caused the entire commercial industry of Shanghai to fall into decline and the economy to fall into bankruptcy, it can be said that only these characters in the attic rooms are most affected. The more the danger of the closure of shops and factories deepens, the greater their unemployment panic becomes. It is often these characters who suffer the cold treatment of the landlords because they have no money to pay the rent. Thus, in the rent reduction movement, it is clear that they should not only actively participate but also become the vanguard of the movement.

So, why don't they participate?

I think this is due to two wrong ideas: on the part of the people living in attic rooms, they always think that their power is too small and they have no right to intervene. It seems that this is just a direct negotiation between the second landlord and the first landlord and the landlord, and it has the meaning of "waiting"—waiting for the movement to have results and enjoying the benefits without any effort. In addition, on the part of the second landlord, they also think that those people are not important. Their participation or non-participation has nothing to do with them, or even is beneficial to them, so they abandon them.

For the sake of the future of the entire movement and for the sake of the individual interests (whether the second landlord or the person living in the attic room), these two concepts should be corrected immediately. Under the general purpose of rent reduction, there is no conflict of interest between the second landlord and the person living in the attic room. With consistent demands, there must be consistent actions. It is certainly not acceptable to only care about one's own interests and not care about the interests of others, and it is equally unacceptable to wait for others to do well and not move oneself. The result will inevitably be disappointment. As for power, it goes without saying. May I ask, since people living in attic rooms suffer even more than second landlords, how can the number of people living in attic rooms be less than that of second landlords?

Amateur Coffee House

Man in a Hail of Arrows 276

— Ms. Qie

"The process of life" is a series of cruel and continuous wars, and the entire "life" is a vast battlefield.

Every day, every day, "life" is attacking people fiercely, without any rest. "Life" is a great military strategist, and it adopts a strategy of both offense and defense, and uses a tactic of attacking from the front and back. In front of people, it has set up three solid defense lines, the first one is called the "death line," and the other two are the "starvation line" and the "cold line." The fortifications are heavily guarded and carefully arranged to prevent people's counterattack. On this side, it takes the defensive. On the other hand, it also sends several brave and good-fighting generals to lead a large army to advance on three routes of "clothing," "food," and "housing," pressing and threatening people from behind. On this side, it takes the offensive. In this way, people have become turtles in a jar, and the whole body is surrounded by the heavy troops of "life"!

However, there is an exception here. "Life" does not dare to invade those few lucky ones, because those lucky ones, they are not afraid of "life" and avoid "life." What are they afraid of! They have money as weapons and wealth as a backing. Western-style houses are the Great Wall to resist "life," fields are their base of operations, bills of exchange are spread all over the world like proclamations, and checks are flying around the streets like declarations of war. "Life" is not their opponent at all. They do not need to be enemies with "life," nor do they need to worry about the pressure of "life"; and, in fact, they also need "life." They welcome it, love it, and do not hesitate to use a lot of money to supply it, satisfy it, and make it reach the highest degree of enjoyment. As for "life" itself, you should know that it is not only a military strategist, but also a conspirator. It bullies the weak and helps the strong, and suppresses the poor and aids the rich. As long as the desires of "life" itself are filled, and it overflows and exceeds needs, why should it persecute them?

However, in the eyes of the remaining majority of people, "life" is really too scary—it wears a helmet, is covered in armor, has a treasure knife hanging from its waist, holds a丈八long spear, and is full of murderous aura and full of majesty. The more you want to run away in panic, the more it chases you. Even when it encounters those five or six-year-old scavenger children who have just come into contact with "life," it takes the lead as if facing a formidable enemy, and even shakes its spirits and yells, "The first general is 'life,' see who dares to come and die!" The cruel war has begun like this!

Many, many people are shot to death by "life" in a hail of arrows, but there are still many, many people fighting bloody battles and carrying out a long-term resistance. They are driven by the three armies of "clothing," "food," and "housing" from behind. They have no other choice but to rush forward, trying to break through the terrible "death line" in front and break out a path to survival. Some of them use up all their strength to cross this first defense line, and then struggle on the "starvation line" and the "cold line," and even further overcome "life" and avenge "life," but on the one hand, they still have to be vigilant at any time against the return of "life." There are also some people who have failed because their environment is too difficult. They have been ambushed by "poverty"; when they are fighting with "life," "poverty" colludes with "life" and stands on the same front as "life" and is their enemy. In this way, even if some of them temporarily defeat "life," they are still defeated by it in the end; some are permanently stuck on the "death line," permanently stuck on the "starvation line" and the "cold line," and are deadlocked with "life"; there are also some who finally become prisoners of "life" and are persecuted and sacrificed by it, and there are more than millions of such people! Really, "life" is the most cruel thing. It is a liar, it is not what it seems, it only has a beautiful and empty slogan; its banner clearly says "life" in big letters, but what it leaves for people is often only a dead end!

The society is becoming more and more depressed, and the economic panic is deepening day by day. Therefore, the defense line of "life" is becoming more and more solid, and the fortifications of "life" are becoming higher and thicker. The fierce firepower of "life" is also becoming more and more concentrated on people. It is really not easy for a troubled person to escape its siege and avoid its sharp edge!
